It receives tool calls from Claude, does the smart work (positioning, layout, text measurement, template expansion), then writes primitives into PG.\n\n## Files to read\n\n1. `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench/docs/ILLUSTRATOR-PRIMITIVES.md` — all 39 MCP tools with parameters\n2. `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench/docs/ILLUSTRATOR-GRAPHICS.md` — graphic element properties and SVG rendering\n3. `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/mcp-illustrator/src/handlers.ts` — current tool handler implementations (business logic)\n4. `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/mcp-illustrator/src/positioning.ts` — relative positioning engine\n5. `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/mcp-illustrator/src/tree.ts` — tree traversal helpers\n6. `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/mcp-illustrator/src/fonts.ts` — text measurement\n7. `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/mcp-illustrator/src/layout.ts` — layout analysis\n8. `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/mcp-illustrator/src/documents.ts` — current document state management\n\n## What to spec\n\n### 1. Tool → PG mapping\n\nFor each of the 39 tools, define the exact orchestration:\n\n```\nadd_text(args) →\n  1. Pack: resolve relative position (below, center_h, etc.) → concrete x, y\n  2. Pack: measure text width if maxWidth (opentype.js)\n  3. PG:   INSERT INTO document.element (canvas_id, type='text', x, y, props={...})\n  4. Return: element id + position summary\n```\n\nDo this for ALL 39 tools. Group by category:\n- Document CRUD (doc_new, doc_save, doc_load, doc_list, doc_delete, doc_duplicate, doc_rename)\n- Canvas (canvas_setup)\n- Element creation (add_text, add_image, add_rect, add_line)\n- Element mutation (update_element, batch_update, delete_element, element_duplicate, reorder_element, clear_canvas)\n- Groups (group_elements, ungroup, add_to_group, remove_from_group)\n- Alignment (align, distribute)\n- Batch (batch_add, batch_update)\n- State (get_state, measure_text, check_layout)\n- Export (export_svg, export_pdf, snapshot)\n- Meta (update_meta)\n- Assets (list_assets)\n- Collaboration (inspect_store, dispatch_event, get_event_log, show_message)\n\n### 2. What lives WHERE\n\nFor each piece of logic, specify:\n- **PG function** — if it's pure data manipulation (CRUD, queries)\n- **Pack (TypeScript)** — if it needs external libs (opentype.js, resvg, pdf-lib) or complex algorithms\n- **Client (browser)** — if it needs user interaction (drag, snap, image editor)\n- **Supabase Realtime** — if it needs push to client\n\n### 3. PG functions needed\n\nList every PL/pgSQL function that `document` module needs:\n```sql\ndocument.create_canvas(name, format, orientation, bg) RETURNS uuid\ndocument.add_element(canvas_id, type, x, y, width, height, props) RETURNS uuid\ndocument.update_element(element_id, props) RETURNS void\ndocument.delete_element(element_id) RETURNS void\ndocument.batch_add(canvas_id, elements jsonb) RETURNS uuid[]\ndocument.batch_update(updates jsonb) RETURNS void\ndocument.reorder(element_id, action text) RETURNS void\ndocument.group_elements(canvas_id, element_ids uuid[], name) RETURNS uuid\ndocument.ungroup(group_id) RETURNS void\ndocument.clear_canvas(canvas_id) RETURNS void\ndocument.get_state(canvas_id) RETURNS jsonb\ndocument.render_svg(canvas_id) RETURNS text\n... etc\n```\n\n### 4. State management pattern\n\nThe current illustrator keeps documents in memory (SQLite + Map). The new architecture is stateless per-request:\n\n```\nEach MCP tool call:\n  1. Read current state from PG (SELECT elements WHERE canvas_id = $1)\n  2. Compute (positioning, layout, measurement)\n  3. Write result to PG (INSERT/UPDATE elements)\n  4. Supabase Realtime auto-pushes changes to client\n```\n\nSpec how this works for:\n- Single element add (simple INSERT)\n- Relative positioning (need to read other elements first to compute position)\n- Batch operations (transaction wrapping)\n- get_state (read-only, format for Claude's context window)\n- align/distribute (read all → compute deltas → batch update)\n\n### 5. Collaboration protocol\n\nMap the current WebSocket protocol to Supabase Realtime:\n\n- State sync: Postgres Changes on document.element → client auto-refreshes\n- Selection sync: Broadcast channel for ephemeral state\n- Toast: Broadcast\n- inspect_store / dispatch_event / get_event_log: Broadcast request/response\n\nHow does the pack send a Broadcast message from an Edge Function?\n\n### 6. Template + data binding orchestration\n\nThe template engine flow:\n```\nTemplate (canvas with elements containing {{merge_fields}})\n  + Data (jsonb from module's *_data(id) function)\n  → Clone canvas\n  → Resolve merge fields in text elements\n  → Expand repeating sections\n  → Evaluate conditions\n  → Compute layout (flow, page breaks)\n  → Output: new canvas with concrete elements\n```\n\nWhat functions are needed? Where do they live (PG or pack)?\n\n## Deliverable\n\nA spec document with:\n1. Complete tool → orchestration mapping (all 39 tools)\n2. PG function catalog (name, signature, what it does)\n3. Pack function catalog (what stays in TypeScript and why)\n4. State management protocol (per-request stateless flow)\n5. Collaboration protocol (Realtime mapping)\n6. Template generation pipeline\n7. 8;\n    42→  const fontFamily = args.fontFamily ?? \"Libre Baskerville\";\n    43→  const fontWeight = args.fontWeight ?? \"bold\";\n    44→  const fontStyle = args.fontStyle ?? \"normal\";\n    45→  const maxWidth = args.maxWidth ?? null;\n    46→  const lines = wrapText(args.text, maxWidth, fontSize, fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle);\n    47→  const tw = Math.max(\n    48→    ...lines.map((l) => measureTextWidth(l, fontSize, fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle)),\n    49→  );\n    50→  const th = fontSize * lines.length * 1.3;\n    51→  return { w: tw, h: th };\n    52→}\n    53→\n    54→/**\n    55→ * Resolve relative positioning params into concrete x/y values.\n    56→ * Returns resolved coordinates to merge into the element args.\n    57→ * Throws on errors (missing reference, no coordinates resolved).\n    58→ */\n    59→export function resolvePosition(\n    60→  doc: Document,\n    61→  type: string,\n    62→  args: any,\n    63→): ResolvedPos {\n    64→  const rel: RelativeArgs = {\n    65→    below: args.below,\n    66→    above: args.above,\n    67→    right_of: args.right_of,\n    68→    left_of: args.left_of,\n    69→    gap: args.gap ?? 0,\n    70→    center_h: args.center_h,\n    71→    center_v: args.center_v,\n    72→  };\n    73→\n    74→  const gap = rel.gap!;\n    75→  const canvas = doc.canvas;\n    76→  const result: ResolvedPos = {};\n    77→  const isLine = type === \"line\";\n    78→  const hasRelative = rel.below || rel.above || rel.right_of || rel.left_of;\n    79→\n    80→  // Get reference element bbox if relative positioning is used\n    81→  let refBox: BBox | undefined;\n    82→  let refEl: Element | undefined;\n    83→  const refName = rel.below || rel.above || rel.right_of || rel.left_of;\n    84→  if (refName) {\n    85→    refEl = findRef(doc, refName);\n    86→    if (!refEl) throw new Error(`Reference element not found: \"${refName}\"`);\n    87→    refBox = bbox(refEl);\n    88→  }\n    89→\n    90→  // ---- Vertical axis (below / above) ----\n    91→  if (rel.below && refBox) {\n    92→    const targetY = refBox.y + refBox.h + gap;\n    93→    if (isLine) {\n    94→      // offset y1/y2\n    95→      result.y1 = targetY + (args.y1 ?? 0);\n    96→      result.y2 = targetY + (args.y2 ?? 0);\n    97→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n    98→      // text y is baseline: add fontSize*0.85\n    99→      result.y = targetY + (args.fontSize ?? 8) * 0.85;\n   100→    } else {\n   101→      result.y = targetY;\n   102→    }\n   103→  }\n   104→\n   105→  if (rel.above && refBox) {\n   106→    if (isLine) {\n   107→      const lineH = Math.abs((args.y2 ?? 0) - (args.y1 ?? 0));\n   108→      const targetY = refBox.y - gap - lineH;\n   109→      result.y1 = targetY + (args.y1 ?? 0);\n   110→      result.y2 = targetY + (args.y2 ?? 0);\n   111→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   112→      // text: y is baseline, place so bottom of text aligns above ref\n   113→      result.y = refBox.y - gap;\n   114→    } else {\n   115→      // rect/image: place so bottom edge is at ref.y - gap\n   116→      const h = args.height ?? 0;\n   117→      result.y = refBox.y - gap - h;\n   118→    }\n   119→  }\n   120→\n   121→  // ---- Horizontal axis (right_of / left_of) ----\n   122→  if (rel.right_of && refBox) {\n   123→    const targetX = refBox.x + refBox.w + gap;\n   124→    if (isLine) {\n   125→      result.x1 = targetX + (args.x1 ?? 0);\n   126→      result.x2 = targetX + (args.x2 ?? 0);\n   127→    } else {\n   128→      result.x = targetX;\n   129→    }\n   130→  }\n   131→\n   132→  if (rel.left_of && refBox) {\n   133→    if (isLine) {\n   134→      const lineW = Math.abs((args.x2 ?? 0) - (args.x1 ?? 0));\n   135→      const targetX = refBox.x - gap - lineW;\n   136→      result.x1 = targetX + (args.x1 ?? 0);\n   137→      result.x2 = targetX + (args.x2 ?? 0);\n   138→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   139→      // text width depends on anchor\n   140→      const dims = textDims(args);\n   141→      const anchor = args.textAnchor ?? \"start\";\n   142→      if (anchor === \"end\") {\n   143→        result.x = refBox.x - gap;\n   144→      } else if (anchor === \"middle\") {\n   145→        result.x = refBox.x - gap - dims.w / 2;\n   146→      } else {\n   147→        result.x = refBox.x - gap - dims.w;\n   148→      }\n   149→    } else {\n   150→      const w = args.width ?? 0;\n   151→      result.x = refBox.x - gap - w;\n   152→    }\n   153→  }\n   154→\n   155→  // ---- Inherit orthogonal axis from reference ----\n   156→  if (refBox && refEl) {\n   157→    if ((rel.below || rel.above) && result.x == null && args.x == null && !rel.center_h && !isLine) {\n   158→      // Inherit x from reference element\n   159→      if (type === \"text\" && \"x\" in refEl) {\n   160→        result.x = (refEl as any).x;\n   161→      } else if (\"x\" in refEl) {\n   162→        result.x = (refEl as any).x;\n   163→      } else {\n   164→        result.x = refBox.x;\n   165→      }\n   166→    }\n   167→    if ((rel.right_of || rel.left_of) && result.y == null && args.y == null && !rel.center_v && !isLine) {\n   168→      // Inherit y from reference element\n   169→      if (\"y\" in refEl) {\n   170→        result.y = (refEl as any).y;\n   171→      } else {\n   172→        result.y = refBox.y;\n   173→      }\n   174→    }\n   175→    // For lines: inherit orthogonal axis as offset\n   176→    if (isLine && (rel.below || rel.above) && result.x1 == null && args.x1 == null) {\n   177→      if (\"x1\" in refEl) {\n   178→        result.x1 = (refEl as any).x1;\n   179→        result.x2 = (refEl as any).x2;\n   180→      } else {\n   181→        result.x1 = refBox.x;\n   182→        result.x2 = refBox.x + refBox.w;\n   183→      }\n   184→    }\n   185→    if (isLine && (rel.right_of || rel.left_of) && result.y1 == null && args.y1 == null) {\n   186→      if (\"y1\" in refEl) {\n   187→        result.y1 = (refEl as any).y1;\n   188→        result.y2 = (refEl as any).y2;\n   189→      } else {\n   190→        result.y1 = refBox.y;\n   191→        result.y2 = refBox.y + refBox.h;\n   192→      }\n   193→    }\n   194→  }\n   195→\n   196→  // ---- Canvas centering ----\n   197→  if (rel.center_h) {\n   198→    if (isLine) {\n   199→      const x1 = result.x1 ?? args.x1 ?? 0;\n   200→      const x2 = result.x2 ?? args.x2 ?? 0;\n   201→      const lineW = Math.abs(x2 - x1);\n   202→      const offset = (canvas.w - lineW) / 2 - Math.min(x1, x2);\n   203→      result.x1 = x1 + offset;\n   204→      result.x2 = x2 + offset;\n   205→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   206→      const anchor = args.textAnchor ?? \"start\";\n   207→      if (anchor === \"middle\") {\n   208→        result.x = canvas.w / 2;\n   209→      } else if (anchor === \"end\") {\n   210→        const dims = textDims(args);\n   211→        result.x = canvas.w / 2 + dims.w / 2;\n   212→      } else {\n   213→        const dims = textDims(args);\n   214→        result.x = (canvas.w - dims.w) / 2;\n   215→      }\n   216→    } else {\n   217→      const w = args.width ?? 0;\n   218→      result.x = (canvas.w - w) / 2;\n   219→    }\n   220→  }\n   221→\n   222→  if (rel.center_v) {\n   223→    if (isLine) {\n   224→      const y1 = result.y1 ?? args.y1 ?? 0;\n   225→      const y2 = result.y2 ?? args.y2 ?? 0;\n   226→      const lineH = Math.abs(y2 - y1);\n   227→      const offset = (canvas.h - lineH) / 2 - Math.min(y1, y2);\n   228→      result.y1 = y1 + offset;\n   229→      result.y2 = y2 + offset;\n   230→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   231→      const dims = textDims(args);\n   232→      result.y = (canvas.h - dims.h) / 2 + (args.fontSize ?? 8) * 0.85;\n   233→    } else {\n   234→      const h = args.height ?? 0;\n   235→      result.y = (canvas.h - h) / 2;\n   236→    }\n   237→  }\n   238→\n   239→  // ---- Explicit args always win ----\n   240→  // For non-line types, if x or y was explicitly provided and no relative override happened,\n   241→  // keep them. The caller should merge result over args, so we only set result if computed.\n   242→  // For lines: explicit x1/y1/x2/y2 are kept unless overridden above.\n   243→\n   244→  return result;\n   245→}\n   246→\n   247→/**\n   248→ * Check if relative positioning args are present\n   249→ */\n   250→export function hasRelativeArgs(args: any): boolean {\n   251→  return !!(args.below || args.above || args.right_of || args.left_of || args.center_h || args.center_v);\n   252→}\n   253→\n   254→// ---- Align ----\n   255→\n   256→type AlignAxis = \"left\" | \"center_h\" | \"right\" | \"top\" | \"center_v\" | \"bottom\";\n   257→\n   258→interface AlignArgs {\n   259→  ids: string[];\n   260→  axis: AlignAxis;\n   261→}\n   262→\n   263→interface ElementDelta {\n   264→  id: string;\n   265→  props: Record<string, number>;\n   266→}\n   267→\n   268→export function computeAlign(doc: Document, args: AlignArgs): ElementDelta[] {\n   269→  const elements = args.ids.map((idOrName) => {\n   270→    const el = findRef(doc, idOrName);\n   271→    if (!el) throw new Error(`Element not found: \"${idOrName}\"`);\n   272→    return el;\n   273→  });\n   274→\n   275→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   276→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   277→\n   278→  switch (args.axis) {\n   279→    case \"left\": {\n   280→      const target = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x));\n   281→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   282→        const dx = target - box.x;\n   283→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   284→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   285→      }\n   286→      break;\n   287→    }\n   288→    case \"right\": {\n   289→      const target = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x + b.box.w));\n   290→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   291→        const dx = target - (box.x + box.w);\n   292→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   293→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   294→      }\n   295→      break;\n   296→    }\n   297→    case \"center_h\": {\n   298→      const minX = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x));\n   299→      const maxR = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x + b.box.w));\n   300→      const center = (minX + maxR) / 2;\n   301→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   302→        const elCenter = box.x + box.w / 2;\n   303→        const dx = center - elCenter;\n   304→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   305→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   306→      }\n   307→      break;\n   308→    }\n   309→    case \"top\": {\n   310→      const target = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y));\n   311→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   312→        const dy = target - box.y;\n   313→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   314→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   315→      }\n   316→      break;\n   317→    }\n   318→    case \"bottom\": {\n   319→      const target = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y + b.box.h));\n   320→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   321→        const dy = target - (box.y + box.h);\n   322→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   323→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   324→      }\n   325→      break;\n   326→    }\n   327→    case \"center_v\": {\n   328→      const minY = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y));\n   329→      const maxB = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y + b.box.h));\n   330→      const center = (minY + maxB) / 2;\n   331→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   332→        const elCenter = box.y + box.h / 2;\n   333→        const dy = center - elCenter;\n   334→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   335→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   336→      }\n   337→      break;\n   338→    }\n   339→  }\n   340→\n   341→  return deltas;\n   342→}\n   343→\n   344→// ---- Distribute ----\n   345→\n   346→interface DistributeArgs {\n   347→  ids: string[];\n   348→  axis?: \"x\" | \"y\";\n   349→  gap?: number;\n   350→  grid?: {\n   351→    cols: number;\n   352→    col_gap: number;\n   353→    row_gap: number;\n   354→    start_x?: number;\n   355→    start_y?: number;\n   356→  };\n   357→}\n   358→\n   359→export function computeDistribute(doc: Document, args: DistributeArgs): ElementDelta[] {\n   360→  const elements = args.ids.map((idOrName) => {\n   361→    const el = findRef(doc, idOrName);\n   362→    if (!el) throw new Error(`Element not found: \"${idOrName}\"`);\n   363→    return el;\n   364→  });\n   365→\n   366→  if (args.grid) {\n   367→    return distributeGrid(elements, args.grid);\n   368→  }\n   369→\n   370→  const axis = args.axis ?? \"y\";\n   371→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   372→\n   373→  // Sort by position on axis\n   374→  boxes.sort((a, b) =>\n   375→    axis === \"x\" ? a.box.x - b.box.x : a.box.y - b.box.y,\n   376→  );\n   377→\n   378→  const n = boxes.length;\n   379→  if (n < 2) return [];\n   380→\n   381→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   382→\n   383→  if (axis === \"x\") {\n   384→    const totalSize = boxes.reduce((s, b) => s + b.box.w, 0);\n   385→    let gap: number;\n   386→    let startX: number;\n   387→\n   388→    if (args.gap != null) {\n   389→      gap = args.gap;\n   390→      startX = boxes[0].box.x;\n   391→    } else {\n   392→      const extent = boxes[n - 1].box.x + boxes[n - 1].box.w - boxes[0].box.x;\n   393→      gap = (extent - totalSize) / (n - 1);\n   394→      startX = boxes[0].box.x;\n   395→    }\n   396→\n   397→    let currentX = startX;\n   398→    for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   399→      const dx = currentX - box.x;\n   400→      if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) {\n   401→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   402→      }\n   403→      currentX += box.w + gap;\n   404→    }\n   405→  } else {\n   406→    const totalSize = boxes.reduce((s, b) => s + b.box.h, 0);\n   407→    let gap: number;\n   408→    let startY: number;\n   409→\n   410→    if (args.gap != null) {\n   411→      gap = args.gap;\n   412→      startY = boxes[0].box.y;\n   413→    } else {\n   414→      const extent = boxes[n - 1].box.y + boxes[n - 1].box.h - boxes[0].box.y;\n   415→      gap = (extent - totalSize) / (n - 1);\n   416→      startY = boxes[0].box.y;\n   417→    }\n   418→\n   419→    let currentY = startY;\n   420→    for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   421→      const dy = currentY - box.y;\n   422→      if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   423→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   424→      }\n   425→      currentY += box.h + gap;\n   426→    }\n   427→  }\n   428→\n   429→  return deltas;\n   430→}\n   431→\n   432→function distributeGrid(\n   433→  elements: Element[],\n   434→  grid: { cols: number; col_gap: number; row_gap: number; start_x?: number; start_y?: number },\n   435→): ElementDelta[] {\n   436→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   437→  const startX = grid.start_x ?? boxes[0].box.x;\n   438→  const startY = grid.start_y ?? boxes[0].box.y;\n   439→\n   440→  // Compute max dimensions per column and row for uniform grid\n   441→  const cols = grid.cols;\n   442→  const maxColW = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.w));\n   443→  const maxRowH = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.h));\n   444→\n   445→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   446→\n   447→  for (let i = 0; i < boxes.length; i++) {\n   448→    const col = i % cols;\n   449→    const row = Math.floor(i / cols);\n   450→    const targetX = startX + col * (maxColW + grid.col_gap);\n   451→    const targetY = startY + row * (maxRowH + grid.row_gap);\n   452→\n   453→    const { el, box } = boxes[i];\n   454→    const dx = targetX - box.x;\n   455→    const dy = targetY - box.y;\n   456→\n   457→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01 || Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   458→      deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, dy));\n   459→    }\n   460→  }\n   461→\n   462→  return deltas;\n   463→}\n   464→\n   465→// ---- Shared: apply delta to raw coordinates ----\n   466→\n   467→function applyDelta(el: Element, dx: number, dy: number): ElementDelta {\n   468→  const props: Record<string, number> = {};\n   469→  if (el.type === \"line\") {\n   470→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) {\n   471→      props.x1 = r(el.x1 + dx);\n   472→      props.x2 = r(el.x2 + dx);\n   473→    }\n   474→    if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   475→      props.y1 = r(el.y1 + dy);\n   476→      props.y2 = r(el.y2 + dy);\n   477→    }\n   478→  } else {\n   479→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) props.x = r((el as any).x + dx);\n   480→    if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) props.y = r((el as any).y + dy);\n   481→  }\n   482→  return { id: el.id, props };\n   483→}\n   484→\n   485→function r(v: number): number {\n   486→  return Math.round(v * 10) / 10;\n   487→}\n   488→"}]},"uuid":"72890a77-ecd1-4adb-854c-f489e9583481","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:40:48.941Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"d04830df-0805-439c-a03f-48bb0a9f7054","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}

Math.max(...lines.map((l) => measureTextWidth(l, el.fontSize, el.fontFamily, el.fontWeight, el.fontStyle)))\n    24→        : Math.max(...lines.map((l) => l.length)) * el.fontSize * 0.55;\n    25→      const th = el.fontSize * lines.length * 1.3;\n    26→      let tx = el.x;\n    27→      if (el.textAnchor === \"middle\") tx -= tw / 2;\n    28→      else if (el.textAnchor === \"end\") tx -= tw;\n    29→      const ty = el.y - el.fontSize * 0.85;\n    30→      return { x: tx, y: ty, w: tw, h: th };\n    31→    }\n    32→    case \"group\": {\n    33→      const children = (el as GroupElement).children;\n    34→      if (!children.length) return { x: 0, y: 0, w: 0, h: 0 };\n    35→      let minX = Infinity, minY = Infinity, maxX = -Infinity, maxY = -Infinity;\n    36→      for (const child of children) {\n    37→        const cb = bbox(child);\n    38→        minX = Math.min(minX, cb.x);\n    39→        minY = Math.min(minY, cb.y);\n    40→        maxX = Math.max(maxX, cb.x + cb.w);\n    41→        maxY = Math.max(maxY, cb.y + cb.h);\n    42→      }\n    43→      return { x: minX, y: minY, w: maxX - minX, h: maxY - minY };\n    44→    }\n    45→    default:\n    46→      return { x: 0, y: 0, w: 0, h: 0 };\n    47→  }\n    48→}\n    49→\n    50→export interface ColorWarning {\n    51→  id: string;\n    52→  type: string;\n    53→  property: string;\n    54→  value: string;\n    55→  reason: string;\n    56→}\n    57→\n    58→export interface LayoutReport {\n    59→  structuralLayers: string[];\n    60→  overlaps: any[];\n    61→  outOfBounds: any[];\n    62→  bleedZone: any[];\n    63→  spacingGroups: any[];\n    64→  colorWarnings: ColorWarning[];\n    65→}\n    66→\n    67→export function checkLayout(\n    68→  d: Document,\n    69→  bleed: number,\n    70→  spaceTol: number,\n    71→  sizeTol: number,\n    72→): LayoutReport {\n    73→  const { w: cW, h: cH } = d.canvas;\n    74→\n    75→  const leaves = flattenLeaves(d.elements);\n    76→  const boxes = leaves.map((el) => ({ id: el.id, type: el.type, bbox: bbox(el), el }));\n    77→\n    78→  // Structural layer detection\n    79→  const canvasArea = cW * cH;\n    80→  const isStructural = (b: typeof boxes[0]) => {\n    81→    const area = b.bbox.w * b.bbox.h;\n    82→    if (area > canvasArea * 0.5) return true;\n    83→    if (b.type === \"rect\" && (b.el.opacity ?? 1) < 1 && (b.bbox.w >= cW * 0.95 || b.bbox.h >= cH * 0.95)) return true;\n    84→    return false;\n    85→  };\n    86→  const structuralIds = new Set(boxes.filter(isStructural).map((b) => b.id));\n    87→\n    88→  // 1. Pairwise overlaps (skip structural layers)\n    89→  const overlaps: any[] = [];\n    90→  for (let i = 0; i < boxes.length; i++) {\n    91→    for (let j = i + 1; j < boxes.length; j++) {\n    92→      if (structuralIds.has(boxes[i].id) || structuralIds.has(boxes[j].id)) continue;\n    93→      const a = boxes[i].bbox, b = boxes[j].bbox;\n    94→      const ix = Math.max(a.x, b.x);\n    95→      const iy = Math.max(a.y, b.y);\n    96→      const ix2 = Math.min(a.x + a.w, b.x + b.w);\n    97→      const iy2 = Math.min(a.y + a.h, b.y + b.h);\n    98→      if (ix < ix2 && iy < iy2) {\n    99→        const iw = Math.round((ix2 - ix) * 10) / 10;\n   100→        const ih = Math.round((iy2 - iy) * 10) / 10;\n   101→        overlaps.push({\n   102→          a: boxes[i].id,\n   103→          b: boxes[j].id,\n   104→          a_type: boxes[i].type,\n   105→          b_type: boxes[j].type,\n   106→          intersection: { x: Math.round(ix * 10) / 10, y: Math.round(iy * 10) / 10, w: iw, h: ih },\n   107→          area_mm2: Math.round(iw * ih * 10) / 10,\n   108→        });\n   109→      }\n   110→    }\n   111→  }\n   112→\n   113→  // 2. Out of bounds\n   114→  const outOfBounds: any[] = [];\n   115→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   116→    const { x, y, w, h } = b.bbox;\n   117→    const sides: any[] = [];\n   118→    if (x < 0) sides.push({ side: \"left\", overflow_mm: Math.round(-x * 10) / 10 });\n   119→    if (y < 0) sides.push({ side: \"top\", overflow_mm: Math.round(-y * 10) / 10 });\n   120→    if (x + w > cW) sides.push({ side: \"right\", overflow_mm: Math.round((x + w - cW) * 10) / 10 });\n   121→    if (y + h > cH) sides.push({ side: \"bottom\", overflow_mm: Math.round((y + h - cH) * 10) / 10 });\n   122→    for (const s of sides) outOfBounds.push({ id: b.id, ...s });\n   123→  }\n   124→\n   125→  // 3. Bleed zone\n   126→  const bleedZone: any[] = [];\n   127→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   128→    const { x, y, w, h } = b.bbox;\n   129→    if (w >= cW * 0.95 && h >= cH * 0.95) continue;\n   130→    const sides: any[] = [];\n   131→    if (x > 0 && x < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"left\", distance_mm: Math.round(x * 10) / 10 });\n   132→    if (y > 0 && y < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"top\", distance_mm: Math.round(y * 10) / 10 });\n   133→    if (x + w < cW && cW - (x + w) < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"right\", distance_mm: Math.round((cW - x - w) * 10) / 10 });\n   134→    if (y + h < cH && cH - (y + h) < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"bottom\", distance_mm: Math.round((cH - y - h) * 10) / 10 });\n   135→    for (const s of sides) bleedZone.push({ id: b.id, ...s });\n   136→  }\n   137→\n   138→  // 4. Spacing groups\n   139→  const spacingGroups: any[] = [];\n   140→  const sizeKey = (b: typeof boxes[0]) => `${b.type}_${Math.round(b.bbox.w / sizeTol) * sizeTol}_${Math.round(b.bbox.h / sizeTol) * sizeTol}`;\n   141→  const groups = new Map<string, typeof boxes>();\n   142→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   143→    const k = sizeKey(b);\n   144→    if (!groups.has(k)) groups.set(k, []);\n   145→    groups.get(k)!.push(b);\n   146→  }\n   147→  for (const [, members] of groups) {\n   148→    if (members.length < 3) continue;\n   149→    const ys = members.map((m) => m.bbox.y);\n   150→    const ySpread = Math.max(...ys) - Math.min(...ys);\n   151→    const xs = members.map((m) => m.bbox.x);\n   152→    const xSpread = Math.max(...xs) - Math.min(...xs);\n   153→\n   154→    if (xSpread > ySpread) {\n   155→      const sorted = [...members].sort((a, b) => a.bbox.x - b.bbox.x);\n   156→      const gaps: number[] = [];\n   157→      for (let i = 1; i < sorted.length; i++) {\n   158→        gaps.push(Math.round((sorted[i].bbox.x - sorted[i - 1].bbox.x - sorted[i - 1].bbox.w) * 10) / 10);\n   159→      }\n   160→      const avgGap = gaps.reduce((s, g) => s + g, 0) / gaps.length;\n   161→      const uniform = gaps.every((g) => Math.abs(g - avgGap) <= spaceTol);\n   162→      spacingGroups.push({\n   163→        ids: sorted.map((m) => m.id),\n   164→        type: members[0].type,\n   165→        axis: \"horizontal\",\n   166→        gaps_mm: gaps,\n   167→        avg_gap_mm: Math.round(avgGap * 10) / 10,\n   168→        uniform,\n   169→      });\n   170→    } else {\n   171→      const sorted = [...members].sort((a, b) => a.bbox.y - b.bbox.y);\n   172→      const gaps: number[] = [];\n   173→      for (let i = 1; i < sorted.length; i++) {\n   174→        gaps.push(Math.round((sorted[i].bbox.y - sorted[i - 1].bbox.y - sorted[i - 1].bbox.h) * 10) / 10);\n   175→      }\n   176→      const avgGap = gaps.reduce((s, g) => s + g, 0) / gaps.length;\n   177→      const uniform = gaps.every((g) => Math.abs(g - avgGap) <= spaceTol);\n   178→      spacingGroups.push({\n   179→        ids: sorted.map((m) => m.id),\n   180→        type: members[0].type,\n   181→        axis: \"vertical\",\n   182→        gaps_mm: gaps,\n   183→        avg_gap_mm: Math.round(avgGap * 10) / 10,\n   184→        uniform,\n   185→      });\n   186→    }\n   187→  }\n   188→\n   189→  // 5. CMYK color warnings\n   190→  const colorWarnings: ColorWarning[] = [];\n   191→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   192→    const el = b.el;\n   193→    const colorProps: [string, string | undefined][] = [\n   194→      [\"fill\", (el as any).fill],\n   195→      [\"stroke\", (el as any).stroke],\n   196→      [\"borderColor\", (el as any).borderColor],\n   197→      [\"shadowColor\", (el as any).shadowColor],\n   198→    ];\n   199→    for (const [prop, val] of colorProps) {\n   200→      if (!val || val === \"none\") continue;\n   201→      if (/^rgba?\\s*\\(/.test(val) && /,\\s*[\\d.]+\\s*\\)$/.test(val) && !/,\\s*1\\s*\\)$/.test(val)) {\n   202→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Transparence (alpha) non supportée en CMJN\" });\n   203→      }\n   204→      if (/^hsla?\\s*\\(/.test(val)) {\n   205→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Couleur HSL — convertir en hex pour l'impression\" });\n   206→      }\n   207→      if (val === \"#000000\" || val === \"#000\" || val.toLowerCase() === \"black\") {\n   208→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Noir pur — utiliser un noir riche (ex: #1C1C1C) pour l'impression\" });\n   209→      }\n   210→      // Detect highly saturated colors likely out of CMYK gamut\n   211→      const hex = parseHex(val);\n   212→      if (hex) {\n   213→        const [r, g, _b] = hex;\n   214→        const max = Math.max(r, g, _b);\n   215→        const min = Math.min(r, g, _b);\n   216→        if (max === 255 && min === 0 && (r === 0 || g === 0 || _b === 0)) {\n   217→          colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Couleur très saturée — hors gamut CMJN probable\" });\n   218→        }\n   219→      }\n   220→    }\n   221→  }\n   222→\n   223→  return { structuralLayers: [...structuralIds], overlaps, outOfBounds, bleedZone, spacingGroups, colorWarnings };\n   224→}\n   225→\n   226→function parseHex(val: string): [number, number, number] | null {\n   227→  const m3 = val.match(/^#([0-9a-f])([0-9a-f])([0-9a-f])$/i);\n   228→  if (m3) return [parseInt(m3[1] + m3[1], 16), parseInt(m3[2] + m3[2], 16), parseInt(m3[3] + m3[3], 16)];\n   229→  const m6 = 43→export function resolveClientResponse(reqId: string, data: any): void {\n    44→  const entry = pending.get(reqId);\n    45→  if (!entry) return;\n    46→  clearTimeout(entry.timer);\n    47→ {"parentUuid":"6f38fe19-71fd-4e47-8413-f2f305508c33","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"93b2ef26-6365-4536-b096-9853760a749b","agentId":"a8cb9e7087b2106a1","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01NkLhMN395VffxynxtmFfjD","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# ILLUSTRATOR.md — Integration MCP Illustrator\n     2→\n     3→> Moteur de rendu documentaire pour la plateforme pgView.\n     4→> MCP Illustrator est le composant de composition et d'export PDF pour tous les documents : devis, factures, brochures produits, communication.\n     5→\n     6→## Vision\n     7→\n     8→Deux mondes, un seul moteur de rendu :\n     9→\n    10→```\n    11→+------------------------------------------------------------------+\n    12→|  pgView (PostgreSQL)           |  MCP Illustrator                |\n    13→|  ============================  |  ============================== |\n    14→|  Affichage web interactif      |  Documents imprimables (PDF)    |\n    15→|  get_devis() -> HTML browser   |  Composition A4 -> PDF 300 DPI  |\n    16→|  Navigation, CRUD, workflow    |  Brochures, catalogues, com'    |\n    17→|  Temps reel, Alpine.js shell   |  Export pro, bleed, crop marks  |\n    18→+------------------------------------------------------------------+\n    19→                  |                              |\n    20→                  +--------- bridge -------------+\n    21→                  |                              |\n    22→          Donnees metier (PL/pgSQL)     Layout (Illustrator tools)\n    23→```\n    24→\n    25→pgView genere le HTML pour le navigateur. Illustrator compose les documents pour l'impression et l'export. Les donnees viennent du meme endroit : PostgreSQL.\n    26→\n    27→## Pourquoi Illustrator (pas un moteur HTML-to-PDF)\n    28→\n    29→Les moteurs HTML-to-PDF (Gotenberg, WeasyPrint, Puppeteer) convertissent du HTML en PDF. Ca marche, mais :\n    30→\n    31→| | HTML-to-PDF | Illustrator |\n    32→|---|------------|-------------|\n    33→| Controle layout | CSS @page, limites navigateur | Millimetrique, pixel-perfect |\n    34→| Typographie | Approximative (navigateur) | Precise (opentype.js, mesure glyphes) |\n    35→| Images | Contraintes CSS | Crop, zoom, filtres, ombres |\n    36→| Bleed / crop marks | Hack ou impossible | Natif, configurable |\n    37→| Brochures / com' | Hors scope | Use case principal |\n    38→| Template reutilisable | HTML + CSS a maintenir | Document clonable |\n    39→| UI de design | Aucune | Editeur web interactif |\n    40→| Clients potentiels | Aucun (c'est de l'infra) | Produit vendable separement |\n    41→\n    42→L'argument decisif : Illustrator sert **aussi** pour la communication (brochures, flyers, catalogues produit). Un moteur HTML-to-PDF ne fait que de la conversion — Illustrator est un outil de creation.\n    43→\n    44→## Architecture d'integration\n    45→\n    46→### Composants\n    47→\n    48→```\n    49→+---------------------------+        +---------------------------+\n    50→|  plpgsql-workbench        |        |  mcp-illustrator          |\n    51→|  (MCP server :3100)       |        |  (MCP server, stdio)      |\n    52→|                           |        |                           |\n    53→|  pg_query / pg_get        |        |  doc_new / doc_duplicate  |\n    54→|  -> donnees metier        |        |  batch_add / batch_update |\n    55→|                           |        |  export_pdf / snapshot    |\n    56→|  quote.devis_data(id)     |        |                           |\n    57→|  quote.facture_data(id)   |        |  Templates = documents    |\n    58→|  crm.client_data(id)      |        |  stockes dans SQLite      |\n    59→+---------------------------+        +---------------------------+\n    60→              |                                    |\n    61→              +------------- bridge ---------------+\n    62→              |                                    |\n    63→     +------------------+                          |\n    64→     |  Orchestrateur   |  (agent Claude, MCP tool, ou script)\n    65→     |  1. Query data   |\n    66→     |  2. Clone template|\n    67→     |  3. Fill data     |\n    68→     |  4. Export PDF    |\n    69→     +------------------+\n    70→```\n    71→\n    72→### Flux de generation\n    73→\n    74→```\n    75→1. QUERY     pg_query(\"SELECT quote.devis_data(42)\")\n    76→             -> { numero, date, client, lignes[], totaux, mentions[] }\n    77→\n    78→2. CLONE     doc_duplicate(\"tpl-devis-standard\")\n    79→             -> nouveau document \"DEV-2026-042\"\n    80→\n    81→3. FILL      batch_update([\n    82→               { name: \"numero\",     text: \"DEV-2026-042\" },\n    83→               { name: \"date\",       text: \"13 mars 2026\" },\n    84→               { name: \"client-nom\", text: \"Dupont SARL\" },\n    85→               ...\n    86→             ])\n    87→             + generation dynamique du tableau de lignes\n    88→\n    89→4. EXPORT    export_pdf({ format: \"A4\", home_print: true })\n    90→             -> PDF binaire\n    91→\n    92→5. CLEANUP   doc_delete(\"DEV-2026-042\")\n    93→             (ou archivage si besoin de re-generation)\n    94→```\n    95→\n    96→## Templates\n    97→\n    98→### Principe : template = document\n    99→\n   100→Pas de DSL, pas de Jinja, pas de moteur de substitution. Un template est un **document Illustrator standard** avec des elements nommes :\n   101→\n   102→```\n   103→tpl-devis-standard (A4 portrait)\n   104→├── logo              image    (x:15, y:15, w:40, h:20)\n   105→├── entreprise-nom    text     (x:15, y:40, \"ACME SARL\")\n   106→├── entreprise-addr   text     (x:15, y:48, \"12 rue des Lilas...\")\n   107→├── entreprise-siret  text     (x:15, y:62, \"SIRET: 123 456 789 00001\")\n   108→├── entreprise-tva    text     (x:15, y:67, \"TVA: FR12345678900\")\n   109→├── client-nom        text     (x:120, y:40, \"[client]\")\n   110→├── client-addr       text     (x:120, y:48, \"[adresse]\")\n   111→├── titre             text     (x:15, y:90, \"DEVIS DEV-XXXX-XXX\")\n   112→├── date              text     (x:160, y:90, \"[date]\")\n   113→├── validite          text     (x:160, y:96, \"Valide 30 jours\")\n   114→├── table-header      group    (y:110)\n   115→│   ├── col-desc      text     \"Description\"\n   116→│   ├── col-qte       text     \"Qte\"\n   117→│   ├── col-unite     text     \"Unite\"\n   118→│   ├── col-pu        text     \"P.U. HT\"\n   119→│   ├── col-tva       text     \"TVA\"\n   120→│   └── col-total     text     \"Total HT\""}]},"uuid":"1c90c375-ae06-443e-be99-2996fe60e3c1","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:41:24.660Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"6f38fe19-71fd-4e47-8413-f2f305508c33","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}

Le client web est hébergé sur **Supabase**.\n     7→La collaboration passe par **Supabase Realtime** au lieu de WebSocket custom.\n     8→\n     9→```\n    10→┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n    11→│ Claude (Desktop / claude.ai)                           │\n    12→│ MCP Streamable HTTP → Edge Function                    │\n    13→└────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────────┘\n    14→             │\n    15→┌────────────▼───────────────────────────────────────────┐\n    16→│ Supabase Edge Function                                 │\n    17→│ packs/illustrator.ts — 36 outils DSL agent             │\n    18→│ ├── positionnement relatif (below, center_h, gap)      │\n    19→│ ├── batch operations (batch_add, batch_update)         │\n    20→│ ├── layout analysis (check_layout)                     │\n    21→│ ├── text measurement (opentype.js)                     │\n    22→│ └── exports (SVG, PNG, DOCX)                           │\n    23→├────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────────┤\n    24→│            │ SQL (postgres.js)                          │\n    25→│ PostgreSQL │                                           │\n    26→│ ├── cad.drawing (document canvas)                      │\n    27→│ ├── cad.shape (éléments: text, image, rect, line)      │\n    28→│ ├── cad.layer (calques)                                │\n    29→│ ├── illustrator.asset (métadonnées images)             │\n    30→│ └── cad.render_svg() (rendu serveur)                   │\n    31→├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────┤\n    32→│ Realtime   │ Postgres Changes → push au client         │\n    33→│            │ Broadcast → toasts, selection sync         │\n    34→├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────┤\n    35→│ Storage    │ Bucket \"assets\" (images utilisateur)       │\n    36→│            │ Bucket \"exports\" (PDF, SVG, DOCX temp)     │\n    37→├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────┤\n    38→│ Auth       │ OAuth 2.0 (Claude Directory)              │\n    39→└────────────┴───────────────────────────────────────────┘\n    40→             │\n    41→┌────────────▼───────────────────────────────────────────┐\n    42→│ Client Web (Supabase static / Vercel)                  │\n    43→│ ├── D3 SVG canvas (drag, snap, selection)              │\n    44→│ ├── Image editor modal (crop, filters)                 │\n    45→│ ├── Asset library panel (photothèque)                  │\n    46→│ ├── Undo/redo manager                                  │\n    47→│ ├── State machine (phases: idle → selected → dragging) │\n    48→│ └── supabase-js (Realtime subscribe + Storage URLs)    │\n    49→└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n    50→```\n    51→\n    52→## Les 5 piliers à préserver\n    53→\n    54→### 1. Collaboration bidirectionnelle\n    55→\n    56→**Aujourd'hui** : WebSocket custom + `requestFromClient()` (request/response over WS).\n    57→Claude envoie un message typé au client, le client répond avec `_reqId`.\n    58→\n    59→**Cible** : Supabase Realtime (Broadcast channel).\n    60→- Canal `doc-{drawingId}` : Postgres Changes sur cad.drawing + cad.shape\n    61→- Canal `collab-{drawingId}` : Broadcast pour selection sync, toasts, inspect\n    62→\n    63→**Équivalences** :\n    64→\n    65→| Aujourd'hui (WS) | Cible (Realtime) |\n    66→|-------------------|------------------|\n    67→| `{ type: \"state\", doc, docList }` | Postgres Changes sur drawing/shape |\n    68→| `{ type: \"select_element\", id }` | Broadcast `{ event: \"select\", elementId }` |\n    69→| `{ type: \"select_asset\", path }` | Broadcast `{ event: \"select_asset\", path }` |\n    70→| `{ type: \"toast\", text, level }` | Broadcast `{ event: \"toast\", text, level }` |\n    71→| `requestFromClient(\"inspect\")` | Broadcast request + response pattern |\n    72→| `requestFromClient(\"dispatch\")` | Broadcast `{ event: \"dispatch\", payload }` |\n    73→| `{ type: \"reload\" }` | N/A (pas de hot reload en prod) |\n    74→\n    75→### 2. Éditeur complet standalone\n    76→\n    77→Le client D3/SVG reste quasi-identique. Changements :\n    78→- **WS → supabase-js Realtime** : remplacer `ws.send()` par `channel.send()`\n    79→- **State sync** : le client écoute Postgres Changes au lieu de `{ type: \"state\" }`\n    80→- **Mutations** : le client appelle PostgREST (`/rpc/add_shape`, `/rpc/move_shape`) au lieu de WS\n    81→- **Assets** : `fetch(\"/api/assets\")` → `supabase.storage.from(\"assets\").list()`\n    82→\n    83→### 3. Asset management intelligent\n    84→\n    85→**Principe fondamental** : les images (blobs) ne transitent **jamais** par le MCP.\n    86→Le MCP ne manipule que des IDs, URLs signées, et métadonnées texte (~100-500 bytes/appel).\n    87→\n    88→**Aujourd'hui** : `assets/` filesystem + `metadata.json` statique.\n    89→\n    90→**Cible** : Supabase Storage (blobs) + table PG (métadonnées) + classification par Claude (vision).\n    91→\n    92→#### Flux upload & classification\n    93→\n    94→```\n    95→1. UPLOAD (client web → Supabase, sans MCP)\n    96→   Client web → Supabase Storage (upload direct, signed URL)\n    97→   Client web → INSERT illustrator.asset (filename, path, status: 'to_classify')\n    98→   L'image lourde ne passe que entre le navigateur et Storage.\n    99→\n   100→2. CLASSIFICATION (Claude via MCP, texte léger uniquement)\n   101→   Claude → list_assets status:'to_classify'          (~100 bytes/asset)\n   102→   Claude → get_asset_url id:123                       → URL signée (~200 bytes)\n   103→   Claude → [vision multimodale] regarde l'image via l'URL\n   104→   Claude → classify_asset id:123                      (~500 bytes)\n   105→            tags:['jazz','concert'] description:'Saxophoniste sur scène'\n   106→            width:1920 height:1080 orientation:'paysage'\n   107→\n   108→3. resolved by parameter name via Awilix PROXY mode.\n     6→ */\n     7→\n     8→import { createContainer, asValue, type AwilixContainer } from \"awilix\";\n     9→import type { McpServer } from \"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js\";\n    10→import type { RequestHandlerExtra } from \"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/shared/protocol.js\";\n    11→import type { ServerRequest, ServerNotification } from \"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/types.js\";\n    12→import type { DbClient } from \"./connection.js\";\n    13→import type { ToolResult } from \"./helpers.js\";  // used by ToolHandler\n    14→import { z } from \"zod\";\n    15→\n    16→// --- Core types ---\n    17→\n    18→export type WithClient = <T>(fn: (client: DbClient) => Promise<T>) => Promise<T>;\n    19→\n    20→/** MCP extra context passed to tool handlers (signal, sendNotification, etc.). */\n    21→export type ToolExtra = RequestHandlerExtra<ServerRequest, ServerNotification>;\n    22→\n    23→export interface ToolMetadata {\n    24→  name: string;\n    25→  description: string;\n    26→  schema: z.ZodObject<any>;\n    27→}\n    28→\n    29→export interface ToolHandler {\n    30→  metadata: ToolMetadata;\n    31→  handler: (args: Record<string, unknown>, extra: ToolExtra) => Promise<ToolResult>;\n    32→}\n    33→\n    34→/** A pack registers services and tools into the container. */\n    35→export type ToolPack = (container: AwilixContainer, config: Record<string, unknown>) => void;\n    36→\n    37→/** Profile: which packs to load + their config. */\n    38→export interface WorkbenchProfile {\n    39→  packs: Record<string, Record<string, unknown>>;\n    40→}\n    41→\n    42→// --- Container builder ---\n    43→\n    44→export function buildContainer(profile: WorkbenchProfile, packs: Record<string, ToolPack>): AwilixContainer {\n    45→  const container = createContainer({ strict: true });\n    46→\n    47→  // Register each requested pack\n    48→  for (const [name, config] of Object.entries(profile.packs)) {\n    49→    const pack = packs[name];\n    50→    if (!pack) throw new Error(`Unknown pack: ${name}`);\n    51→    pack(container, config);\n    52→  }\n    53→\n    54→  // Resolve only tool registrations (named *Tool) to avoid eagerly creating\n    55→  // infrastructure like the DB pool at startup.\n    56→  const registry = new Map<string, ToolHandler>();\n    57→  for (const name of Object.keys(container.registrations)) {\n    58→    if (!name.endsWith(\"Tool\")) continue;\n    59→    const val = container.resolve(name);\n    60→    if (isToolHandler(val)) {\n    61→      registry.set(val.metadata.name, val);\n    62→    }\n    63→  }\n    64→\n    65→  container.register({\n    66→    toolRegistry: asValue(registry),\n    67→  });\n    68→\n    69→  return container;\n    70→}\n    71→\n    72→// --- MCP mounting ---\n    73→\n    74→/**\n    75→ * Register tools from the container onto an McpServer.\n    76→ * In dev mode (WORKBENCH_MODE=dev or Text Primitives\n    16→\n    17→Text is the foundation of every business document. The current engine has basic single-style text with word-wrap. Business and creative documents demand far more.\n    18→\n    19→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n    20→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n    21→| 1.1 | **Single-line text** | Positioned text with font, size, color, anchor | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`add_text`) |\n    22→| 1.2 | **Multi-line text (word-wrap)** | Auto-wrap to maxWidth, explicit `\\n` breaks | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`maxWidth`) |\n    23→| 1.3 | **Text alignment** | start/middle/end (horizontal anchor) | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`textAnchor`) |\n    24→| 1.4 | **Rich text spans** | Bold, italic, color changes within a single text block. E.g. \"Total: **1 480,80 EUR**\" | MUST | 1 | H | MISSING -- currently entire block shares one style |\n    25→| 1.5 | **Paragraph text** | Multi-paragraph blocks with inter-paragraph spacing, first-line indent | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING -- `\\n` exists but no paragraph-level control |\n    26→| 1.6 | **Justified text** | Full justification (left+right aligned) via Knuth-Plass or greedy algorithm | SHOULD | 2 | H | MISSING |\n    27→| 1.7 | **Multi-column text** | Text flowing across 2-3 columns (brochures, newsletters) | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    28→| 1.8 | **Bulleted lists** | Bullet character + hanging indent, nested levels | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    29→| 1.9 | **Numbered lists** | Auto-incrementing numbers/letters, nested levels | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    30→| 1.10 | **Merge fields / variables** | `{{client.name}}`, `{{facture.total}}` -- placeholder syntax resolved at generation time | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING -- currently done by orchestrator via `batch_update`, but no native support |\n    31→| 1.11 | **Text overflow: shrink-to-fit** | Auto-reduce font size if text exceeds bounding box | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    32→| 1.12 | **Text overflow: truncate + ellipsis** | Clip text with \"...\" when exceeding maxWidth | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n    33→| 1.13 | **Text overflow: linked frames** | Text overflowing from one frame continues in another (multi-page) | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    34→| 1.14 | **Superscript / subscript** | For legal references (1), footnote markers, chemical formulas | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    35→| 1.15 | **Text decorations** | Underline, strikethrough, overline | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n    36→| 1.16 | **RTL / BiDi text** | Right-to-left (Arabic, Hebrew), bidirectional mixing | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    37→| 1.17 | **CJK text** | Chinese/Japanese/Korean vertical and horizontal layout | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    38→| 1.18 | **Hyphenation** | Automatic word hyphenation per language rules (essential for justified text) | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    39→\n    40→### Analysis\n    41→\n    42→The biggest gap for business documents is **1.4 Rich text spans** -- every invoice needs \"Total TTC: **1 480,80 EUR**\" with the amount in bold. Without this, generating professional documents requires multiple separate text elements positioned manually, which is fragile.\n    43→\n    44→**1.10 Merge fields** is architecturally important: currently the orchestrator does batch_update after cloning a template, which works but means Claude must understand every field mapping. A native `{{variable}}` system would make templates self-documenting and enable non-AI generation pipelines.\n    45→\n    46→---\n    47→\n    48→## 2. Table Primitives\n    49→\n    50→Tables are the heart of business documents. Every invoice, quote, purchase order, and report has at least one. The current engine has **no table primitive** -- tables must be composed from individual text and line elements.\n    51→\n    52→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n    53→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n    54→| 2.1 | **Simple table** | Rows, columns, cells with text content | MUST | 1 | H | MISSING -- composed manually from text+lines |\n    55→| 2.2 | **Header row** | Distinct styling (bold, background), repeated on page break | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING |\n    56→| 2.3 | **Column widths: fixed** | Explicit width per column in mm | MUST | 1 | L | MISSING |\n    57→| 2.4 | **Column widths: proportional** | Star-sizing (`*`, `2*`, `3*`) to fill available width | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    58→| 2.5 | **Column widths: auto** | Shrink to content width | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    59→| 2.6 | **Cell alignment** | Horizontal (left, center, right) and vertical (top, middle, bottom) per cell | MUST | 1 | L | MISSING |\n    60→| 2.7 | **Cell borders** | Per-side border control (top, right, bottom, left), style (solid, dashed), width, color | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING |\n    61→| 2.8 | **Cell merge: colspan** | Cell spanning multiple columns | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    62→| 2.9 | **Cell merge: rowspan** | Cell spanning multiple rows | SHOULD | 2 | H | MISSING |\n    63→| 2.10 | **Alternating row colors** | Zebra striping for readability | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n    64→| 2.11 | **Table footer row** | Summary/totals row with distinct styling | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n    65→| 2.12 | **Table page break** | Table splits across pages with header repeated | MUST | 1 | H | MISSING (requires multi-page) |\n    66→| 2.13 | **Nested content in cells** | Images, sub-tables, rich text within cells | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    67→| 2.14 | **Row grouping** | Collapsible sections within a table (report subtotals) | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n    68→| 2.15 | **Cell padding** | Inner spacing between cell border and content | MUST | 1 | L | MISSING |\n    69→\n    70→### Analysis\n    71→\n    72→Tables are the **single biggest gap** for business document generation. Building an invoice table from individual positioned text elements requires ~6 elements per row, manual Y calculation, and breaks completely on multi-page documents. A native table primitive is the highest priority addition.\n    73→\n    74→The minimum viable table needs: rows/columns, header row, fixed column widths, cell alignment, cell borders, cell padding. This alone unblocks 80% of business documents.\n    75→\n    76→---\n    77→\n    78→## 3. Let me produce the full architecture spec.\n\n---\n\n# Illustrator Orchestration Layer — Architecture Blueprint\n\n## 1. Patterns and Conventions Found\n\n**DI Container pattern** (`/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench/src/core/container.ts:44`)\nEvery pack is a function `(container: AwilixContainer, config) => void`. Tools are named `*Tool` and auto-discovered. Pack registers infrastructure services first, then tool factories that declare dependencies as named destructured parameters.\n\n**Tool factory pattern** (`/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench/src/core/packs/plpgsql.ts:41`)\n`createXxxTool({ withClient, ... }: Deps): ToolHandler`. `ToolHandler` = `{ metadata: { name, description, schema }, handler }`.\n\n**WithClient abstraction** (`/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench/src/core/drivers/supabase.ts:24`)\n`WithClient = (fn: (client: DbClient) => Promise<T>) => Promise<T>`. The Edge Function uses `createPostgresWithClient(sql)` where `sql` is a `postgres.js` instance pointed at `SUPABASE_DB_URL`.\n\n**LMNAV output format** (`/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench/src/core/helpers.ts`)\n`text(string)` for plain results. LMNAV conventions: key-value pairs, `->` arrows, no JSON wrapping, navigable IDs. The `compactState()` function in handlers.ts is the model for `get_state` output.\n\n**Current mutable state model** (`/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/mcp-illustrator/src/documents.ts:19`)\nIn-memory `Map<string, Document>` + SQLite. The migration replaces both with PostgreSQL as the single source of truth.\n\n**Positioning engine** (`/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/mcp-illustrator/src/positioning.ts:59`)\nPure function `resolvePosition(doc, type, args) -> ResolvedPos`. Needs canvas dimensions + sibling element bboxes. Both are available per-request via a `SELECT`.\n\n**Bus events** (`/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/mcp-illustrator/src/bus.ts:7`)\nEvents that currently go to the WS bridge become Supabase Realtime Broadcast messages on channel `collab-{drawing_id}`.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Architecture Decision\n\n**Stateless per-request with PG as single source of truth.** Each MCP tool call:\n1. Opens a transaction via `withClient`\n2. Reads the current canvas state from `document.canvas` + `document.element` (only what it needs — typically just for positioning computation)\n3. Executes the Pack's TypeScript logic (positioning, measurement, bbox, align deltas)\n4. Writes result to PG in the same transaction\n5. Broadcasts a Realtime event on the `collab-{canvas_id}` channel (fire-and-forget, outside the transaction)\n6. Returns an LMNAV-formatted response to Claude\n\n**Why not pure PG for everything:** `opentype.js` text measurement, `resvg` PNG rendering, and `pdf-lib`/puppeteer PDF generation cannot run in PG. Everything that touches these libraries stays in the pack TypeScript. Everything that is pure data manipulation belongs in PG functions.\n\n**The PG schema is `document`, not `cad`.** The migration plan mentions reusing `cad.drawing/shape`, but `cad` is a bounded context for 3D wood structures. The illustrator needs its own schema to avoid coupling and to support illustrator-specific props (crop, filters, shadow, merge fields) without polluting `cad`. The schema is named `document`.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Component Design\n\n### 3.1 File Tree\n\n```\nsrc/core/\n├── packs/\n│   └── illustrator.ts               -- Awilix pack (registers all services + tools)\n├── tools/illustrator/\n│   ├── positioning.ts               -- resolvePosition(), hasRelativeArgs(), bbox()\n│   ├── fonts.ts                     -- loadFonts(), measureTextWidth(), wrapText()\n│   ├── layout.ts                    -- checkLayout(), bbox() alias for external use\n│   ├── tree.ts                      -- findInTree(), flattenLeaves(), reassignIds()\n│   ├── svg.ts                       -- buildSVG(elements, canvas) -> string\n│   ├── realtime.ts                  -- sendBroadcast(supabaseUrl, anonKey, channel, event)\n│   ├── state.ts                     -- loadCanvas(), compactState(),            -- createAddImageTool\n│   ├── add-rect.ts                  -- createAddRectTool\n│   ├── add-line.ts                  -- createAddLineTool\n│   ├── update-element.ts            -- createBatchAddTool\n│   ├── get-state.ts                 -- createGetStateTool\n│   ├── measure-text.ts              -- createMeasureTextTool\n│   ├── check-layout.ts              --
