createSnapshotTool\n│   ├── update-meta.ts               -- createUpdateMetaTool\n│   ├── list-assets.ts               -- createListAssetsTool\n│   ├── inspect-store.ts             -- createInspectStoreTool\n│   ├── dispatch-event.ts            -- createDispatchEventTool\n│   ├── get-event-log.ts             -- createGetEventLogTool\n│   └── show-message.ts              -- createShowMessageTool\n\nmodules/document/\n├── module.json\n├── build/\n│   ├── document.ddl.sql             -- schema + tables + indexes + grants\n│   └── document.func.sql            -- all PG functions (pg_pack output)\n└── src/\n    └── document/\n        ├── canvas_create.sql\n        ├── canvas_update.sql\n        ├── element_add.sql\n        ├── element_update.sql\n        ├── element_delete.sql\n        ├── element_batch_add.sql\n        ├── element_batch_update.sql\n        ├── element_reorder.sql\n        ├── element_duplicate.sql\n        ├── group_create.sql\n        ├── group_dissolve.sql\n        ├── group_add_member.sql\n        ├── group_remove_member.sql\n        ├── canvas_clear.sql\n        ├── canvas_get_state.sql\n        ├── canvas_render_svg.sql\n        ├── asset_list.sql\n        ├── asset_classify.sql\n        ├── asset_get_url.sql\n        ├── asset_delete.sql\n        └── document_list.sql\n```\n\n### 3.2 The Pack (`src/core/packs/illustrator.ts`)\n\n```typescript\nexport const illustratorPack: ToolPack = (container, config) => {\n  // Infrastructure\n  container.register({\n    supabaseUrl: asValue(config.supabaseUrl ?? Deno.env.get(\"SUPABASE_URL\")),\n    supabaseAnonKey: asValue(config.supabaseAnonKey ?? Deno.env.get(\"SUPABASE_ANON_KEY\")),\n    supabaseServiceKey: asValue(config.supabaseServiceKey ?? Deno.env.get(\"SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY\")),\n    sendBroadcast: asFunction(({ supabaseUrl, supabaseServiceKey }) =>\n      makeSendBroadcast(supabaseUrl, supabaseServiceKey)\n    ).singleton(),\n    loadedFonts: asValue(loadFonts()),   // eager: loads TTF files once\n  });\n\n  // Tool registrations (each ending in Tool for auto-discovery)\n  container.register({\n    docNewTool: asFunction(createDocNewTool),\n    docSaveTool: asFunction(createDocSaveTool),\n    // ... all 36 tools\n  });\n};\n```\n\nThe pack depends on `withClient` already being registered by the `plpgsql` pack (or an equivalent in the Supabase Edge Function context where `createPostgresWithClient` is used).\n\n### 3.3 The Shared State Loader (`src/core/tools/illustrator/state.ts`)\n\nThis module is used by nearly every tool. Its job is to load the full canvas state from PG into a `Document` object that is structurally identical to the existing `types.ts` shapes, so all existing `positioning.ts`, `layout.ts`, and `tree.ts` logic runs unchanged.\n\n```typescript\nexport interface LoadedCanvas {\n  canvas_id: string;\n  canvas: Canvas;\n  elements: Element[];\n  meta: DocMeta;\n  name: string;\n  category: string;\n}\n\nexport async function loadCanvas(client: DbClient, canvasId: string): Promise<LoadedCanvas>\n// SELECT c.*, json_agg(e ORDER BY e.z_order) as elements\n// FROM document.canvas c LEFT JOIN document.element e ON e.canvas_id = c.id\n// WHERE c.id = $1 GROUP BY c.id\n\nexport async function resolveCanvasId(client: DbClient, nameOrId: string): Promise<string | null>\n// SELECT id FROM document.canvas WHERE id = $1 OR name = $1 LIMIT 1\n\nexport function toDocument(loaded: LoadedCanvas): Document\n// Adapts PG rows to the existing Document shape for use in positioning/layout/tree\n\nexport function compactState(loaded: LoadedCanvas): string\n// LMNAV format: header + elements tree, same layout as existing compactState()\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Tool to PG Mapping — Complete Catalog\n\n### Document CRUD\n\n**`doc_new(name, format, orientation, background, category)`**\n- Pack: compute `w`, `h` from format + orientation (FORMATS table, screen format detection)\n- PG: `document.canvas_create(name, format, orientation, w, h, bg, category) RETURNS uuid`\n- Broadcast: `{ event: \"document:created\", canvasId }`\n- Return: `New canvas \"{name}\" [{category}] ({format} {orient} {w}x{h}mm)  id: {uuid}`\n\n**`doc_save(name?)`**\n- Pack: resolve active canvas (from session or explicit name), optional rename\n- PG: `document.canvas_rename(canvas_id, new_name) RETURNS void` (if rename) + `document.canvas_touch(canvas_id)` to update `updated_at`\n- Note: there is no \"save\" operation — PG writes are immediate per call. `doc_save` just confirms persistence + optional rename.\n- Broadcast: `{ event: \"document:saved\", canvasId }`\n- Return: `Saved \"{name}\"`\n\n**`doc_load(name_or_id)`**\n- Pack: resolve canvas ID, then `loadCanvas()` to verify it exists\n- PG: `resolveCanvasId()` then nothing else — loading is implicit (state is always in PG)\n- The \"active document\" concept: in a stateless server, there is no global active document. Instead the tool accepts a `canvas_id` or `name` parameter, and operations that need it require it explicitly. **Exception**: for UX continuity, a session token (passed as a query param on the MCP endpoint, stored in an HTTP cookie, or as a `session_id` arg on each tool) maps to a `document.session` table row that stores `active_canvas_id`. See Section 4 (State Management).\n- Return: `Loaded \"{name}\" ({format}, {count} elements)`\n\n**`doc_list(category?)`**\n- Pack: none\n- PG: `document.list_canvases(user_id, category) RETURNS SETOF canvas_summary`\n- Return: LMNAV list: `- {name} [{category}] ({format}, {count} elements, updated {ago})`\n\n**`doc_delete(name_or_id)`**\n- Pack: safety check — refuse if only one canvas exists (port the existing guard)\n- PG: `document.canvas_delete(canvas_id) RETURNS void` (CASCADE deletes all elements)\n- Broadcast: `{ event: \"document:deleted\", canvasId }`\n- Return: `Deleted \"{name}\"`\n\n**`doc_duplicate(name, source?)`**\n- Pack: none\n- PG: `document.canvas_duplicate(source_id, new_name) RETURNS uuid` — deep copy canvas + all elements with new UUIDs, sets new `created_at`\n- Broadcast: `{ event: \"document:created\", canvasId: newId }`\n- Return: `Cloned \"{source}\" -> \"{name}\" ({count} elements)  id: {uuid}`\n\n**`doc_rename(name)`**\n- Pack: none\n- PG: `document.canvas_rename(canvas_id, new_name) RETURNS void` + unique constraint check\n- Broadcast: `{ event: \"document:loaded\", canvasId }` (client reloads title)\n- Return: `Renamed \"{old}\" -> \"{name}\"`\n\n### Canvas\n\n**`canvas_setup(format?, orientation?, background?)`**\n- Pack: recompute `w`, `h` from new format/orientation\n- PG: `document.canvas_update(canvas_id, format, orientation, w, h, bg) RETURNS void`\n- Broadcast: `{ event: \"canvas:changed\", canvasId }`\n- Return: `Canvas: {format} {orient} ({w}x{h}mm) bg={bg}`\n\n### Element Creation\n\n**`add_text(text, x?, y?, below?, above?, right_of?, left_of?, gap?, center_h?, center_v?, fontSize?, fontFamily?, fontWeight?, fontStyle?, fill?, textAnchor?, maxWidth?, opacity?, rotation?, name?, group?)`**\n1. Pack: `loadCanvas(client, canvasId)` to get sibling elements + canvas dims (only if relative args present — `hasRelativeArgs()`)\n2. Pack: `resolvePosition(doc, \"text\", args)` -> `{ x, y }` (unchanged from existing code)\n3. Pack: if `maxWidth`, call `wrapText()` to verify wrap is feasible — no storage needed, just validation\n4. PG: `document.element_add(canvas_id, 'text', z_order_next, props_jsonb) RETURNS uuid`\n   - `props` = `{ x, y, text, fontSize, fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle, fill, textAnchor, maxWidth, opacity, rotation }`\n   - If `group` specified: `document.element_add_to_group(group_id, element_id)`\n5. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:added\", elementId }`\n6. Return: `Text \"{preview}\" -> {id} ({name}) at x:{x} y:{y}`\n\n**`add_image(path?, asset_id?, x?, y?, width, height, below?, ...relative, objectFit?, cropX?, cropY?, cropZoom?, flipH?, flipV?, brightness?, contrast?, grayscale?, borderWidth?, borderColor?, borderRadius?, shadowX?, shadowY?, shadowBlur?, shadowColor?, opacity?, rotation?, name?, group?)`**\n1. Pack: if `path` (legacy local file) — load from filesystem, encode as data URI. If `asset_id` — fetch signed URL from `illustrator.asset` via PG. **Blobs never transit via MCP in production**; only the signed URL is stored in props.\n2. Pack: `resolvePosition()` if relative args\n3. Pack: if `asset_id`, query `document.asset_get_dimensions(asset_id)` for `naturalWidth/Height`\n4. PG: `document.element_add(canvas_id, 'image', z_order_next, props_jsonb) RETURNS uuid`\n   - `props` includes `asset_id`, `storage_url` (signed URL stored at insert time, refreshed at render time), all crop/filter/border/shadow props\n5. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:added\", elementId }`\n6. Return: `Image \"{filename}\" -> {id} at x:{x} y:{y} {w}x{h}mm`\n\n**`add_rect(x?, y?, width, height, fill?, stroke?, strokeWidth?, rx?, opacity?, rotation?, name?, group?, ...relative)`**\n1. Pack: `resolvePosition()` if relative args\n2. PG: `document.element_add(canvas_id, 'rect', z_order_next, props_jsonb) RETURNS uuid`\n3. Broadcast + Return: `Rect -> {id} at x:{x} y:{y} {w}x{h}mm`\n\n**`add_line(x1, y1, x2, y2, stroke?, strokeWidth?, opacity?, rotation?, name?, group?, ...relative)`**\n1. Pack: `resolvePosition(doc, \"line\", args)` for relative args (line has x1/y1/x2/y2 semantics)\n2. PG: `document.element_add(canvas_id, 'line', z_order_next, props_jsonb) RETURNS uuid`\n3. Broadcast + Return: `Line -> {id} ({x1},{y1} -> {x2},{y2})`\n\n### Element Mutation\n\n**`update_element(id, props)`**\n1. Pack: if `props.path` (image path change) — reload image data URI\n2. Pack: if `props.asset_id` — refresh signed URL\n3. PG: `document.element_update(element_id, props_patch_jsonb) RETURNS void`\n   - Uses `props = props || $2` (jsonb merge) not full replace\n4. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:updated\", elementId }`\n5. Return: `Updated {id} ({name})`\n\n**`batch_update(updates: [{id, props}])`**\n1. Pack: for each update where `props.path` or `props.asset_id` — reload image/URL\n2. PG: `document.element_batch_update(updates_jsonb) RETURNS integer` — single transaction, returns count updated\n3. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:updated\", elementId: \"batch\" }`\n4. Return: `Batch updated {count}/{total} elements`\n\n**`delete_element(id)`**\n1. Pack: none\n2. PG: `document.element_delete(element_id) RETURNS jsonb` — returns `{ id, name, type, childCount }` for the response message. Cascades to children if it's a group.\n3. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:deleted\", elementId }`\n4. Return: `Deleted {id} ({name})`\n\n**`element_duplicate(id_or_name, offset_x?, offset_y?)`**\n1. Pack: none\n2. PG: `document.element_duplicate(element_id, offset_x, offset_y) RETURNS uuid` — deep copy, new UUIDs, strips `name` field from clone, applies offset to all coordinates\n3. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:added\", elementId: newId }`\n4. Return: `Duplicated \"{id}\" -> {newId} (offset +{dx},+{dy}mm)`\n\n**`reorder_element(id, action: to_front|to_back|forward|backward)`**\n1. Pack: validate action is one of the four values\n2. PG: `document.element_reorder(element_id, action) RETURNS void` — manipulates `z_order` column within the same parent scope\n3. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:reordered\", elementId, action }`\n4. Return: `Reordered {id} -> {action}`\n\n**`clear_canvas(canvas_id?)`**\n1. Pack: none\n2. PG: `document.canvas_clear(canvas_id) RETURNS integer` — DELETE all elements, returns count\n3. Broadcast: `{ event: \"elements:cleared\", canvasId }`\n4. Return: `Canvas cleared ({count} elements removed)`\n\n### Groups\n\n**`group_elements(ids[], name?)`**\n1. Pack: validate all IDs are siblings (same parent) — requires `loadCanvas()` + tree traversal to find parent arrays; this validation cannot be done efficiently in PG without PL/pgSQL recursion\n2. PG (if validation passes): `document.group_create(canvas_id, element_ids_array, name) RETURNS uuid` — wraps elements in a new group element, preserves z-order\n3. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:added\", elementId: groupId }`\n4. Return: `Grouped {n} elements -> {groupId} ({name})`\n\n**`ungroup(id)`**\n1. Pack: none\n2. PG: `document.group_dissolve(group_id) RETURNS integer` — removes group, promotes children to parent level at same z-position, returns child count\n3. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:updated\", elementId: \"batch\" }`\n4. Return: `Ungrouped {id}: {n} children released`\n\n**`add_to_group(element_id, group_id)`**\n1. Pack: `loadCanvas()` + `isAncestorOf()` cycle check — critical safety validation\n2. PG: `document.group_add_member(group_id, element_id) RETURNS void`\n3. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:updated\", elementId: \"batch\" }`\n4. Return: `Moved {elementId} into group {groupId}`\n\n**`remove_from_group(element_id)`**\n1. Pack: `loadCanvas()` to verify element is inside a group (not already at top level)\n2. PG: `document.group_remove_member(element_id) RETURNS void` — moves element to top-level z_order\n3. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:updated\", elementId: \"batch\" }`\n4. Return: `Removed {elementId} from group -> top level`\n\n### Alignment\n\n**`align(ids[], axis: left|center_h|right|top|center_v|bottom)`**\n1. Pack: `loadCanvas()` to get elements with coordinates\n2. Pack: `computeAlign(doc, { ids, axis })` -> `ElementDelta[]` (unchanged from existing `positioning.ts`)\n3. PG: `document.element_batch_update(deltas_jsonb) RETURNS integer` — same function as batch_update but with coordinate-only patches\n4. Broadcast: `{ event: \"element:updated\", elementId: \"batch\" }`\n5. Return: `Aligned {n} elements on {axis} ({moved} moved)`\n\n**`distribute(ids[], axis?, gap?, grid?)`**\n1. Pack: `loadCanvas()` + `computeDistribute(doc, args)` -> `ElementDelta[]`\n2. PG: `document.element_batch_update(deltas_jsonb) RETURNS integer`\n3. Broadcast + Return: `Distributed {n} elements ({mode}, {moved} moved)`\n\n### Batch\n\n**`batch_add(elements[])`**\n- Pack: iterate the elements array, calling the corresponding pack-level add logic for each (resolve positions sequentially — each element can reference previous elements by name, so positions must be resolved in order)\n- Critical: this runs sequentially, not in parallel. Each element is resolved after the previous is committed to PG, because `below: \"prev-element-name\"` needs the previous element's PG row to exist and be loadable.\n- PG: each element calls its respective `document.element_add()`\n- Return: multi-line LMNAV with one line per added element\n\n### State\n\n**`get_state(canvas_id?, format?: compact|full)`**\n1. Pack: `loadCanvas(client, canvasId)`\n2. Pack: `compactState(loaded)` (LMNAV format) or `JSON.stringify(sanitizeElements(loaded))` for full format\n3. No writes, no broadcast\n4. Return: LMNAV document tree or JSON\n\n**`measure_text(text, fontSize, fontFamily?, fontWeight?, fontStyle?, maxWidth?)`**\n1. Pack: `wrapText()` + `measureTextWidth()` using loaded opentype fonts\n2. No PG access, no broadcast — pure computation\n3. Return: LMNAV with lines count, width, height, line preview\n\n**`check_layout(canvas_id?, bleed_mm?, spacing_tolerance_mm?, size_tolerance_mm?)`**\n1. Pack: `loadCanvas()` + `checkLayout(doc, bleed, spaceTol, sizeTol)` -> `LayoutReport`\n2. No writes, no broadcast\n3. Return: LMNAV summary + JSON detail of overlaps/bleed/spacing/color warnings\n\n### Export\n\n**`export_svg(canvas_id?, embed_images?)`**\n1. Option A (preferred): PG: `document.canvas_render_svg(canvas_id, embed_images) RETURNS text` — server-side SVG generation in PL/pgSQL. This is the same logic as `buildSVG()` ported to SQL. Images are referenced by Storage URLs, not base64-embedded in PG storage.\n2. Option B (fallback): Pack: `loadCanvas()` then TypeScript `buildSVG(elements, canvas)`. Use this if the PG function is too complex to maintain initially.\n3. Return: raw SVG string (MCP text content)\n\n**`export_pdf(canvas_id?, bleed_mm?, crop_marks?, dpi?, home_print?, safe_margin_mm?)`**\n1. Pack: `loadCanvas()` then `buildSVG()` in TypeScript\n2. Pack: `generatePdf(svg, options)` using `pdf-lib` (no Chrome dependency)\n   - `pdf-lib` is pure JS, compatible with Deno/Edge Functions\n   - Puppeteer is incompatible with Edge — it is dropped entirely\n3. Pack: upload PDF to Supabase Storage bucket `exports/` with a signed URL (1 hour TTL)\n4. Return: `PDF exported ({size} KB, {mode})  url: {signedUrl}` — Claude can pass this URL to the user or trigger a download\n\n**`snapshot(canvas_id?, width?)`**\n1. Pack: `loadCanvas()` then TypeScript `buildSVG()`\n2. Pack: `resvg.render()` -> PNG\n3. Pack: return as MCP `image` content type (base64) — same as existing behavior\n4. Return: MCP image content block (Claude displays inline)\n\n### Meta\n\n**`update_meta(canvas_id?, designNotes?, teamNotes?, rating?)`**\n1. Pack: validate `rating` is 0-5\n2. PG: `document.canvas_update_meta(canvas_id, design_notes, team_notes, rating) RETURNS void`\n3. Broadcast: `{ event: \"meta:updated\", canvasId }`\n4. Return: `Meta updated: rating={n}/5, designNotes={n}c, teamNotes={n}c`\n\n### Assets\n\n**`list_assets(status?, tags?, q?)`**\n1. Pack: none\n2. PG: `document.asset_list(user_id, status, tags, q) RETURNS SETOF asset_summary` — FTS on `search_vec` column if `q` present\n3. Return: LMNAV list: `- {id} {filename} [{tags}] {w}x{h} {status}`\n\n### Collaboration\n\n**`inspect_store(slices?)`**\n1. Pack: `sendBroadcast(channel, { event: \"inspect_request\", slices, reqId })` then wait for response on the same channel (broadcast request/response pattern — see Section 5)\n2. Return: LMNAV summary of client state (phase, selected IDs, doc name, element count)\n\n**`dispatch_event(event_type, ...args)`**\n1. Pack: build event payload, `sendBroadcast(channel, { event: \"dispatch_request\", payload, reqId })`\n2. Wait for response\n3. Return: `Dispatched {event_type} -> phase: {phase}, selectedIds: [{ids}]`\n\n**`get_event_log(limit?, filter?, blocked_only?)`**\n1. Pack: `sendBroadcast(channel, { event: \"log_request\", limit, filter, blocked_only, reqId })`\n2. Wait for response\n3. Return: LMNAV event log with timestamps\n\n**`show_message(text, level?, duration?)`**\n1. Pack: `sendBroadcast(channel, { event: \"toast\", text, level, duration })`\n2. Fire-and-forget (no response needed)\n3. Return: `Toast sent: \"{text}\"`\n\n---\n\n## 5. PG Function Catalog\n\nAll functions live in the `document` schema. They are thin — they do data manipulation only, no computation logic that belongs in TypeScript.\n\n```sql\n-- Canvas CRUD\ndocument.canvas_create(name text, format text, orientation text, w numeric, h numeric, bg text, category text) RETURNS uuid\ndocument.canvas_update(canvas_id uuid, format text, orientation text, w numeric, h numeric, bg text) RETURNS void\ndocument.canvas_update_meta(canvas_id uuid, design_notes text, team_notes text, rating int) RETURNS void\ndocument.canvas_rename(canvas_id uuid, new_name text) RETURNS void\ndocument.canvas_touch(canvas_id uuid) RETURNS void                           -- UPDATE updated_at = now()\ndocument.canvas_delete(canvas_id uuid) RETURNS void                          -- CASCADE deletes elements\ndocument.canvas_duplicate(source_id uuid, new_name text) RETURNS uuid        -- deep copy\ndocument.canvas_clear(canvas_id uuid) RETURNS integer                        -- DELETE elements, return count\ndocument.canvas_get_state(canvas_id uuid) RETURNS jsonb                      -- canvas row + ordered elements array\ndocument.canvas_render_svg(canvas_id uuid, embed_images bool) RETURNS text   -- full SVG string\n\n-- Element CRUD\ndocument.element_add(canvas_id uuid, type text, z_order int, props jsonb) RETURNS uuid\ndocument.element_update(element_id uuid, props_patch jsonb) RETURNS void     -- props = props || $2\ndocument.element_delete(element_id uuid) RETURNS jsonb                       -- returns {id, name, type, childCount}\ndocument.element_duplicate(element_id uuid, offset_x numeric, offset_y numeric) RETURNS uuid\ndocument.element_reorder(element_id uuid, action text) RETURNS void          -- to_front/to_back/forward/backward\ndocument.element_batch_add(canvas_id uuid, elements jsonb) RETURNS uuid[]    -- array of element definitions\ndocument.element_batch_update(updates jsonb) RETURNS integer                 -- [{id, props}] array\n\n-- Group operations\ndocument.group_create(canvas_id uuid, element_ids uuid[], name text) RETURNS uuid\ndocument.group_dissolve(group_id uuid) RETURNS integer                       -- returns child count\ndocument.group_add_member(group_id uuid, element_id uuid) RETURNS void\ndocument.group_remove_member(element_id uuid) RETURNS void                   -- moves to top-level\n\n-- Next z_order helper (used by element_add)\ndocument.canvas_next_z_order(canvas_id uuid) RETURNS integer                 -- SELECT max(z_order)+1\n\n-- Asset management\ndocument.asset_list(p_user_id uuid, p_status text, p_tags text[], p_q text) RETURNS SETOF asset_summary\ndocument.asset_classify(p_asset_id uuid, p_tags text[], p_description text, p_title text, p_usage_hint text, p_colors text[]) RETURNS void\ndocument.asset_get_url(p_asset_id uuid) RETURNS text                         -- returns storage path for signed URL generation\ndocument.asset_delete(p_asset_id uuid) RETURNS void\ndocument.asset_get_dimensions(p_asset_id uuid) RETURNS jsonb                 -- {w, h, orientation}\n\n-- Document listing\ndocument.list_canvases(p_user_id uuid, p_category text) RETURNS SETOF canvas_summary\n```\n\n### DDL Schema (`modules/document/build/document.ddl.sql`)\n\n```sql\nCREATE SCHEMA document;\n\nCREATE TABLE document.canvas (\n  id          UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  user_id     UUID,                          -- NULL in dev/single-user mode\n  name        TEXT NOT NULL,\n  category    TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'general',\n  format      TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'A4',\n  orientation TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'portrait',\n  w           NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL,        -- mm\n  h           NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL,        -- mm\n  bg          TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '#ffffff',\n  meta        JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',   -- {designNotes, teamNotes, rating}\n  created_at  TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),\n  updated_at  TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),\n  UNIQUE(user_id, name)\n);\n\nCREATE TABLE document.element (\n  id          UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  canvas_id   UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES document.canvas(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n  parent_id   UUID REFERENCES document.element(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,  -- NULL = top-level\n  type        TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (type IN ('text', 'image', 'rect', 'line', 'group')),\n  z_order     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n  name        TEXT,\n  props       JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',\n  created_at  TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()\n);\n\nCREATE INDEX idx_element_canvas ON document.element(canvas_id, z_order);\nCREATE INDEX idx_element_parent ON document.element(parent_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_element_name   ON document.element(canvas_id, name) WHERE name IS NOT NULL;\n\nCREATE TABLE document.session (\n  id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  user_id         UUID,\n  active_canvas_id UUID REFERENCES document.canvas(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,\n  updated_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()\n);\n\nCREATE TABLE illustrator.asset (\n  -- (as specified in ILLUSTRATOR-MIGRATION.md lines 132-173)\n  id          UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  user_id     UUID,\n  path        TEXT NOT NULL,\n  filename    TEXT NOT NULL,\n  mime_type   TEXT NOT NULL,\n  status      TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'to_classify',\n  width       INTEGER,\n  height      INTEGER,\n  orientation TEXT,\n  title       TEXT,\n  description TEXT,\n  tags        TEXT[],\n  credit      TEXT,\n  saison      TEXT,\n  usage_hint  TEXT,\n  colors      TEXT[],\n  created_at  TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),\n  classified_at TIMESTAMPTZ,\n  search_vec  TSVECTOR GENERATED ALWAYS AS (\n    setweight(to_tsvector('simple', coalesce(title,'')), 'A') ||\n    setweight(to_tsvector('simple', coalesce(description,'')), 'B') ||\n    setweight(to_tsvector('simple', coalesce(array_to_string(tags,' '),'')), 'A')\n  ) STORED\n);\n\n-- Grants\nGRANT USAGE ON SCHEMA document TO web_anon;\nGRANT EXECUTE ON ALL FUNCTIONS IN SCHEMA document TO web_anon;\nGRANT SELECT ON ALL TABLES IN SCHEMA document TO web_anon;\n```\n\n**Key design decisions in the DDL:**\n\nThe `document.element` table uses a flat `parent_id` self-reference instead of storing children in a JSONB array. This means:\n- Groups are elements with `type = 'group'` and their children have `parent_id` pointing to them\n- `canvas_get_state` reconstructs the nested tree in SQL using a recursive CTE\n- `z_order` is scoped per `(canvas_id, parent_id)` — top-level elements share one scope, group children share another\n\nThe `props` JSONB column stores all type-specific properties. No columns for `x`, `y`, `fontSize`, etc. — everything is in `props`. This gives maximum flexibility for future element types without DDL migrations.\n\n---\n\n## 6. Pack Function Catalog (What Stays in TypeScript and Why)\n\n| Function | File | Why TypeScript |\n|----------|------|----------------|\n| `loadFonts()` | `fonts.ts` | Reads `.ttf` files from Edge Function bundle; `opentype.js` is a native JS library with no Deno WASM equivalent |\n| `measureTextWidth(text, size, family, weight, style)` | `fonts.ts` | Requires opentype.js glyph advance width computation |\n| `wrapText(text, maxWidth, ...)` | `fonts.ts` | Depends on `measureTextWidth`; greedy word-wrap loop |\n| `resolvePosition(doc, type, args)` | `positioning.ts` | Requires `bbox()` which requires `measureTextWidth` for text elements; circular dep with PG functions |\n| `hasRelativeArgs(args)` | `positioning.ts` | Pure args inspection, trivial |\n| `computeAlign(doc, {ids, axis})` | `positioning.ts` | Batch coordinate computation over in-memory element array; easier and faster than N PG round-trips |\n| `computeDistribute(doc, args)` | `positioning.ts` | Same as align |\n| `bbox(element)` | `layout.ts` | Requires `measureTextWidth` for text elements; PG cannot call opentype.js |\n| `checkLayout(doc, ...)` | `layout.ts` | Full pairwise overlap detection (O(n²)) with complex bbox logic |\n| `findInTree()` / `flattenLeaves()` | `tree.ts` | Used as input to positioning/layout after `loadCanvas()` materializes the tree |\n| `buildSVG(elements, canvas)` | `svg.ts` | Pure serialization, can run in Edge; PG alternative possible but SVG filter/shadow generation is complex SQL |\n| `generatePdf(svg, options)` | (new) `pdf.ts` | `pdf-lib` is pure JS/Deno-compatible; Puppeteer is incompatible with Edge Functions |\n| `resvg.render(svg)` | `snapshot.ts` | `@resvg/resvg-js` is a compiled WASM module; works in Deno/Edge with the Deno WASM target |\n| `sendBroadcast(channel, event)` | `realtime.ts` | Supabase Realtime REST API call; not available from PG context |\n| `waitForBroadcastResponse(reqId)` | `realtime.ts` | Async request/response over Broadcast; requires in-process promise resolution |\n| `loadCanvas(client, canvasId)` | `state.ts` | Coordination: run PG query + reconstruct nested tree from flat rows + convert to `Document` type |\n\n**What stays in PG:** All CRUD operations, the recursive CTE tree reconstruction for `canvas_get_state`, the SVG renderer (optional: start with TS, move to PG when stable), asset metadata queries, the duplicate deep-copy logic.\n\n---\n\n## 7. State Management Protocol (Stateless Per-Request)\n\nThe key insight is that the \"active document\" session problem must be solved cleanly because the MCP Streamable HTTP transport creates a fresh handler per request — there is no in-process state between calls.\n\n### Session Token Pattern\n\nEach tool call includes a `session_id` parameter (optional, defaults to `\"default\"` in dev). The pack resolves the active canvas via:\n\n```sql\nSELECT active_canvas_id FROM document.session WHERE id = $1\n```\n\nTools that change the active document (`doc_new`, `doc_load`, `doc_duplicate`, `doc_rename`, `doc_delete`) call:\n\n```sql\nUPDATE document.session SET active_canvas_id = $2, updated_at = now() WHERE id = $1\n```\n\nIf `session_id` is not provided, the pack uses the `canvas_id` parameter directly. This means Claude can always work without sessions by passing explicit `canvas_id` values.\n\n### Per-Operation Data Flow\n\n**Single element add (the common case):**\n\n```\nadd_text(text:\"Hello\", below:\"title\", session_id:\"abc\") ->\n\n1. withClient:\n   a. SELECT active_canvas_id FROM document.session WHERE id = 'abc'     -> canvas_id\n   b. IF hasRelativeArgs:\n      SELECT c.w, c.h, json_agg(e ORDER BY e.z_order) as elements\n      FROM document.canvas c JOIN document.element e ON e.canvas_id = c.id\n      WHERE c.id = canvas_id                                               -> LoadedCanvas\n   c. Pack: toDocument(loaded) -> Document object\n   d. Pack: resolvePosition(doc, \"text\", args) -> {x: 42.5, y: 78.3}\n   e. INSERT INTO document.element(canvas_id, type, z_order, props)\n      VALUES (canvas_id, 'text', next_z, $props_jsonb) RETURNING id        -> element_id\n2. sendBroadcast(\"collab-{canvas_id}\", {event:\"element:added\", elementId})\n3. Return: LMNAV response\n```\n\n**Relative positioning requires a single SELECT that loads all elements, not multiple queries.** The `join` in step (b) loads everything at once. The in-memory `Document` object is discarded at the end of the handler — nothing is cached.\n\n**Align / distribute (read-all, compute-deltas, batch-write):**\n\n```\nalign(ids:[\"e1\",\"e2\",\"e3\"], axis:\"left\", canvas_id:\"xyz\") ->\n\n1. withClient (single transaction):\n   a. loadCanvas -> Document (all elements in memory)\n   b. computeAlign(doc, {ids, axis}) -> [{id:\"e1\", props:{x:15}}, ...]\n   c. document.element_batch_update('[{\"id\":\"e1\",\"props\":{\"x\":15}},...]') -> 3\n2. sendBroadcast(...)\n3. Return\n```\n\n**Batch add (sequential with position inheritance):**\n\n```\nbatch_add(elements:[\n  {type:\"text\", name:\"title\", text:\"Hello\", x:15, y:20},\n  {type:\"text\", text:\"World\", below:\"title\", gap:5}\n]) ->\n\n1. withClient (transaction per element, not one big transaction):\n   a. Element 0: no relative args -> INSERT -> id \"e1\"\n   b. Element 1: has \"below:title\" -> loadCanvas() -> find \"title\" by name -> e1 at y:20 ->\n                 resolvePosition -> y = 20 + fontSize*1.3 + 5 -> INSERT -> id \"e2\"\n2. Broadcast each addition\n3. Return multi-line summary\n```\n\nSequential processing is correct here. Wrapping all of `batch_add` in a single transaction would require a single `loadCanvas()` call at the start and then appending each new element to the in-memory Document before the next relative positioning resolution — feasible but more complex. The simpler approach is one transaction per element with sequential PG round-trips. For typical batch sizes (5-20 elements), this is fast enough.\n\n**get_state (read-only):**\n\n```\nget_state(canvas_id:\"xyz\") ->\n\n1. withClient:\n   a. document.canvas_get_state(\"xyz\") -> jsonb {canvas, elements_tree, meta}\n2. Pack: reconstruct Element[] from the jsonb tree (toDocument())\n3. Pack: compactState() -> LMNAV string\n4. Return (no writes, no broadcast)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Collaboration Protocol (Realtime Mapping)\n\n### Channel Architecture\n\nTwo channels per canvas:\n\n- `postgres-changes:document.element:canvas_id=eq.{canvas_id}` — Supabase Postgres Changes, auto-pushes INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE to the client's `supabase-js` subscription. The client receives `{ eventType, new, old }` and reconstructs local state.\n- `broadcast:collab-{canvas_id}` — Supabase Broadcast channel for ephemeral events (toasts, selection sync, inspect).\n\n### Realtime Module (`src/core/tools/illustrator/realtime.ts`)\n\nThe pack sends Broadcast messages via the Supabase REST API from the Edge Function. The Supabase client SDK's Realtime channel must be initialized, but from a server-side Edge Function the correct approach is a direct HTTP call to the Realtime REST endpoint.\n\n```typescript\nexport type BroadcastEvent =\n  | { event: \"toast\"; text: string; level?: string; duration?: number }\n  | { event: \"element:added\"; elementId: string }\n  | { event: \"element:updated\"; elementId: string }\n  | { event: \"element:deleted\"; elementId: string }\n  | { event: \"elements:cleared\"; canvasId: string }\n  | { event: \"canvas:changed\"; canvasId: string }\n  | { event: \"document:created\"; canvasId: string }\n  | { event: \"document:loaded\"; canvasId: string }\n  | { event: \"document:deleted\"; canvasId: string }\n  | { event: \"inspect_request\"; slices?: string[]; reqId: string }\n  | { event: \"dispatch_request\"; payload: object; reqId: string }\n  | { event: \"log_request\"; limit?: number; filter?: string; reqId: string };\n\nexport type SendBroadcast = (canvasId: string, event: BroadcastEvent) => Promise<void>;\n\n// Implementation: POST https://{project}.supabase.co/realtime/v1/api/broadcast\n// with Authorization: Bearer {service_role_key}\n// body: { messages: [{ topic: \"realtime:collab-{canvasId}\", event: event.event, payload: event }] }\n```\n\n### Request/Response Pattern for inspect_store, dispatch_event, get_event_log\n\nThe current WebSocket `requestFromClient()` pattern maps to Broadcast with a `reqId` correlation:\n\n```\nPack (Edge Function):\n  1. Generate reqId = crypto.randomUUID()\n  2. Subscribe to Broadcast channel (collab-{canvasId}) listening for {reqId}_response\n  3. Send Broadcast { event: \"inspect_request\", reqId }\n  4. Wait up to 3s for response\n  5. On response arrival: { event: \"{reqId}_response\", data: {...} } -> resolve\n  6. Unsubscribe\n\nClient:\n  1. Receives inspect_request on collab channel\n  2. Reads local Redux/Zustand state\n  3. Sends Broadcast { event: \"{reqId}_response\", data: {phase, ui, doc, ephemeral} }\n```\n\nThe challenge: subscribing to a Broadcast channel from a Supabase Edge Function requires the `@supabase/supabase-js` client, which works in Deno. However, the latency budget for a 3s timeout is tight for a cold-start Edge Function. The `inspect_store`, `dispatch_event`, and `get_event_log` tools should document that they require an open browser session and will timeout if no client is connected.\n\n---\n\n## 9. Template Generation Pipeline\n\nTemplates are documents with named elements containing `{{merge_field}}` syntax in text content. The generation pipeline runs entirely in the pack layer (TypeScript), not in PG, because it requires text parsing and potentially font measurement for layout reflow.\n\n### Pipeline Steps\n\n```\ntemplate_generate(template_name, data_source, output_name, data?)\n\n1. LOAD TEMPLATE\n   loadCanvas(client, template_name) -> LoadedCanvas (with all {{}} fields)\n\n2. DUPLICATE\n   PG: document.canvas_duplicate(template_id, output_name) -> new_canvas_id\n\n3. LOAD DATA\n   If data_source is a PG function name:\n     withClient: SELECT {data_source}(data_id) -> jsonb\n   Else if data is provided directly:\n     Use data parameter\n\n4. RESOLVE MERGE FIELDS (Pack, TypeScript)\n   Walk element tree (flattenLeaves())\n   For each text element:\n     resolved = resolveTemplate(el.text, data)  -- {{client.name}} -> \"Dupont SARL\"\n   If resolved differs: collect update delta\n\n5. EXPAND REPEATING SECTIONS (Pack)\n   Detect group elements with props.repeat_source = \"data.lignes\"\n   For each item in data[repeat_source]:\n     Clone the group, resolve merge fields with item data\n     Position below previous clone (using below/gap logic)\n   Remove the template group\n\n6. EVALUATE CONDITIONS (Pack)\n   Elements with props.condition = \"data.tva_applicable\"\n   If condition evaluates falsy: delete element from output\n\n7. COMPUTE LAYOUT (Pack)\n   If any repeating sections were expanded: the document height may have changed.\n   For single-page documents: update canvas height to fit content.\n   For multi-page (future): distribute elements across pages.\n\n8. BATCH WRITE\n   PG: document.element_batch_update(all_resolved_elements) RETURNS integer\n   Plus deletes for conditional-false elements\n\n9. RETURN\n   canvas_id: {new_canvas_id}\n   elements_resolved: {count}\n   sections_expanded: {n} repetitions of {m} templates\n   next: [\"export_pdf(canvas_id:{new_canvas_id})\", \"get_state(canvas_id:{new_canvas_id})\"]\n```\n\n### Merge Field Resolution\n\n```typescript\n// src/core/tools/illustrator/template.ts\n\nexport function resolveTemplate(text: string, data: Record<string, any>): string {\n  return text.replace(/\\{\\{([^}]+)\\}\\}/g, (_, path) => {\n    const value = getNestedValue(data, path.trim());\n    return value != null ? String(value) : `{{${path}}}`;  // keep unresolved fields visible\n  });\n}\n\nfunction getNestedValue(obj: any, path: string): any {\n  return path.split(\".\").reduce((v, k) => v?.[k], obj);\n}\n```\n\n### PG Functions for Template Support\n\n```sql\n-- Merge field detection (for tooling/validation)\ndocument.template_fields(canvas_id uuid) RETURNS text[]\n-- Extracts {{field}} patterns from all text elements, returns deduplicated list\n\n-- Generate from template (orchestration wrapper — optional, for non-MCP usage)\ndocument.template_generate(template_id uuid, output_name text, data jsonb) RETURNS uuid\n-- Could be a thin wrapper that calls the pack via pg_net, or left entirely in the pack\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Data Flow Diagrams\n\n### A. add_text with Relative Positioning\n\n```\nClaude -> add_text(text:\"Sous-titre\", below:\"titre\", gap:3, fontSize:10)\n  |\n  v\nillustratorPack.addTextTool.handler(args)\n  |\n  v\nwithClient:\n  1. resolveCanvasId(session_id) -> canvas_id = \"abc-123\"\n  2. hasRelativeArgs? YES (below:\"titre\")\n  3. SELECT canvas.w, canvas.h, json_agg(element ORDER BY z_order)\n     FROM document.canvas JOIN document.element ON canvas_id\n     WHERE canvas.id = 'abc-123'\n     -> {w:210, h:297, elements:[{id:\"e1\", name:\"titre\", type:\"text\", props:{x:15, y:35, fontSize:14}}]}\n  4. Pack: toDocument() -> Document object (in-memory only)\n  5. Pack: resolvePosition(doc, \"text\", {below:\"titre\", gap:3, fontSize:10})\n     -> bbox(\"titre\") = {x:15, y:24.1, w:60, h:18.2}  (y - fontSize*0.85)\n     -> targetY = 24.1 + 18.2 + 3 = 45.3\n     -> text baseline = 45.3 + 10*0.85 = 53.8\n     -> result = {x:15, y:53.8}                       (inherit x from ref)\n  6. SELECT max(z_order)+1 FROM document.element WHERE canvas_id = 'abc-123'  -> 2\n  7. INSERT INTO document.element(canvas_id, type, z_order, props)\n     VALUES ('abc-123', 'text', 2,\n       '{\"x\":15,\"y\":53.8,\"text\":\"Sous-titre\",\"fontSize\":10,...}')\n     RETURNING id -> \"e2\"\n  |\n  v\nsendBroadcast(\"collab-abc-123\", {event:\"element:added\", elementId:\"e2\"})\n  -> POST https://xyz.supabase.co/realtime/v1/api/broadcast  (fire-and-forget)\n  |\n  v\nReturn: text('Text \"Sous-titre\" -> e2 at x:15 y:53.8')\n```\n\n### B. align\n\n```\nClaude -> align(ids:[\"e3\",\"e4\",\"e5\"], axis:\"left\")\n  |\n  v\nwithClient (single transaction):\n  1. loadCanvas(client, canvas_id)\n     SELECT ... json_agg(element ORDER BY z_order) -> 5 elements loaded\n  2. toDocument() -> Document\n  3. computeAlign(doc, {ids:[\"e3\",\"e4\",\"e5\"], axis:\"left\"})\n     -> bbox(e3) = {x:20, y:80, w:40, h:10}\n        bbox(e4) = {x:35, y:95, w:40, h:10}   <- leftmost would be e3 at x:20\n        bbox(e5) = {x:25, y:110, w:40, h:10}\n     -> target_x = min(20,35,25) = 20\n     -> deltas: [{id:\"e4\", props:{x:20}}, {id:\"e5\", props:{x:20}}]\n  4. document.element_batch_update('[{\"id\":\"e4\",\"props\":{\"x\":20}},{\"id\":\"e5\",\"props\":{\"x\":20}}]')\n     -> UPDATE document.element SET props = props || '{\"x\":20}' WHERE id = ... RETURNING count\n     -> 2\n  |\n  v\nsendBroadcast({event:\"element:updated\", elementId:\"batch\"})\n  |\n  v\nReturn: text('Aligned 3 elements on left (2 moved)')\n```\n\n### C. get_state\n\n```\nClaude -> get_state(canvas_id:\"abc-123\")\n  |\n  v\nwithClient (read-only):\n  1. document.canvas_get_state('abc-123')\n     -- Recursive CTE:\n     WITH RECURSIVE tree AS (\n       SELECT id, type, z_order, name, props, parent_id, 0 as depth\n       FROM document.element WHERE canvas_id = 'abc-123' AND parent_id IS NULL\n       UNION ALL\n       SELECT e.id, e.type, e.z_order, e.name, e.props, e.parent_id, t.depth+1\n       FROM document.element e JOIN tree t ON e.parent_id = t.id\n     )\n     SELECT jsonb_build_object(\n       'canvas', to_jsonb(c),\n       'elements', (SELECT jsonb_agg(t ORDER BY t.depth, t.z_order) FROM tree t)\n     ) FROM document.canvas c WHERE c.id = 'abc-123'\n     -> jsonb\n  2. Pack: toDocument(jsonb) -- reconstruct nested Element[] from flat jsonb\n  3. Pack: compactState(doc) -- LMNAV tree format\n  |\n  v\nReturn: LMNAV text (no writes, no broadcast)\n\nOutput format:\n  Canvas: \"Devis DEV-2026-042\" [quote] A4 portrait 210x297mm bg:#ffffff | 14 elements\n  ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n  e1 (logo)          image  x:15 y:15  40x20mm\n  e2 (entreprise-nom) text  \"ACME SARL\" x:15 y:40  sz:10 fill:#1C1C1C\n  e3 (titre)         text  \"DEVIS DEV-2026-042\" x:15 y:90  sz:14 fill:#000000\n  e4 (table-header)  group  [6 children]\n    e5 (col-desc)    text  \"Description\" x:15 y:112  sz:8 fill:#666666\n    ...\n```\n\n### D. Template Generation\n\n```\nClaude -> (sequence of MCP calls for template generation)\n\nStep 1: Claude queries data\n  pg_query(\"SELECT quote.devis_data(42)\") -> json blob\n\nStep 2: Clone template\n  doc_duplicate(source:\"tpl-devis-standard\", name:\"DEV-2026-042\")\n  -> canvas_id = \"new-uuid\"\n\nStep 3: Fill static fields\n  batch_update(canvas_id:\"new-uuid\", updates:[\n    {id:\"e2\", props:{text:\"ACME SARL\"}},\n    {id:\"e3\", props:{text:\"DEV-2026-042\"}},\n    ...12 more fields\n  ])\n\nStep 4: Expand line items (dynamic section)\n  -- Claude builds elements array from data.lignes\n  batch_add(canvas_id:\"new-uuid\", elements:[\n    {type:\"text\", text:\"Installation...\", x:15, y:130, ...},\n    {type:\"text\", text:\"3\", x:120, y:130, ...},\n    {type:\"text\", text:\"1 200,00 €\", x:150, y:130, ...},\n    -- row 2:\n    {type:\"text\", text:\"Câblage...\", x:15, y:142, ...},\n    ...\n  ])\n\nStep 5: Export\n  export_pdf(canvas_id:\"new-uuid\", home_print:true)\n  -> url: https://xyz.supabase.co/storage/v1/object/sign/exports/DEV-2026-042.pdf?token=...\n```\n\nNote: Steps 3-4 are today's \"manual orchestration by Claude\" pattern. The `template_generate` function in Section 9 automates this into a single MCP call for future use, but the current pattern works without any new primitives.\n\n---\n\n## 11. Critical Details\n\n### Error Handling\n\nEvery tool that calls `loadCanvas()` must handle the case where `canvas_id` is null (no active session) or the canvas does not exist. Use the LMNAV error triplet format:\n\n```\nproblem: Canvas not found\nwhere: doc_new argument or session active_canvas_id\nfix_hint: call doc_new to create a canvas or doc_load to load an existing one\n```\n\nPositioning errors from `resolvePosition()` (reference element not found) bubble as `problem: Reference element not found: \"titre\"` — map these to LMNAV format, not TypeScript exceptions propagating to the MCP transport.\n\n### Session Management\n\nIn development (`WORKBENCH_MODE=dev`), use a default session ID `\"dev\"`. In production (Supabase), the session ID comes from the auth JWT's `sub` claim — each user has exactly one session row that tracks their active canvas. The session table acts as a lightweight \"clipboard\" — it is never the source of truth for document state, only for \"which canvas is currently active.\"\n\n### z_order Scoping\n\nThe `z_order` column is scoped per `(canvas_id, parent_id)`. Two elements with the same `parent_id` at the same `z_order` is a conflict. The `canvas_next_z_order(canvas_id, parent_id)` function handles this:\n\n```sql\nCREATE FUNCTION document.canvas_next_z_order(p_canvas_id uuid, p_parent_id uuid DEFAULT NULL) RETURNS integer AS $$\n  SELECT coalesce(max(z_order), 0) + 1\n  FROM document.element\n  WHERE canvas_id = p_canvas_id\n    AND (parent_id = p_parent_id OR (parent_id IS NULL AND p_parent_id IS NULL))\n$$ LANGUAGE sql;\n```\n\n### Image Storage Pattern\n\nImages are never stored in the `props` JSONB as base64. The `props.storage_path` is a Supabase Storage path. At render time (`buildSVG`, `generatePdf`, `snapshot`), the pack generates signed URLs for each image element:\n\n```typescript\nasync function resolveImageUrls(elements: Element[], supabase: SupabaseClient): Promise<Element[]>\n```\n\nSigned URLs are 1-hour TTL. For `export_pdf` and `snapshot`, this is fine. For `export_svg` (which returns the SVG string to Claude), image references are storage paths unless `embed_images: true` is passed, in which case the pack fetches each image and base64-encodes it inline.\n\n### pack.ts Registration Order\n\nIn `illustratorPack`, `loadedFonts` must be registered before any tool that depends on font measurement. Since Awilix resolves lazily, this is fine — but `loadFonts()` loads TTF files synchronously from the filesystem. In the Edge Function context, font files are bundled in the `supabase/functions/` directory at deploy time. Use Deno's `import.meta.url` to resolve the path to the bundled fonts directory.\n\n### Testing Approach\n\nTools are tested via pgTAP for PG functions and via direct `handleTool()` calls (same as the existing `mcp-illustrator` test pattern) for the pack layer. No new test framework needed. The `pg_test` MCP tool runs pgTAP tests against the `document_ut` schema:\n\n```sql\n-- modules/document/src/document_ut/test_element_add.sql\nCREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION document_ut.test_element_add() RETURNS setof text AS $$\nBEGIN\n  -- Setup\n  PERFORM document.canvas_create('test', 'A4', 'portrait', 210, 297, '#fff', 'test');\n  -- ...\n  RETURN NEXT ok(element_id IS NOT NULL, 'element_add returns uuid');\n  RETURN NEXT ok(count = 1, 'element exists in table');\nEND;\n$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;\n```\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Files\n\n**Current mcp-illustrator (source of logic to port):**\n-
